Sixty-Six Countries in the World Implement Economic Truce

The Organizing Committee of the Economic Conference Unanimously Decided

The Truce Period is from Today to the End of August

However, It Can Be Revised in the Event of Drastic Changes in International Exchange Rates

(London) The Organizing Committee of the World Economic Conference unanimously passed the proposal for an economic truce tonight, from today until after August 31st. It can only be revised in the event of drastic changes in international currency prices leading to an emergency situation. Representatives from various countries believe that if the US dollar continues to fall sharply, or if other currencies undergo drastic changes, it will endanger the trade of several countries. France and Italy are particularly concerned about the situation of the US dollar. Therefore, it was decided that if there is a sharp change in currency prices, the British Foreign Secretary Simon will convene an extraordinary meeting of the committee. In addition, the reservation proposed by Japanese Ambassador Matsudaira was accepted after obtaining the approval of his government. Under this condition, the committee unanimously decided to send the minutes of today's meeting to the governments of the sixty-six countries invited to the meeting, hoping that they can all abide by this agreement indefinitely. However, after July 31st, they can withdraw from the truce with one month's notice. According to the members, they had previously sought instructions from their respective governments on this matter, so it is expected that several countries will approve the minutes of this meeting within a few days. According to US news, the financial and official circles have had a good impact on this decision by the organizing committee, and many believe that the economic truce will be of great help to stabilizing exchange rates.

(12th National Telegram)

(London) The Organizing Committee of the World Economic Conference today agreed on a tariff standstill, but with several reservations. After the meeting of the Organizing Committee, a communiqué was issued, strongly urging the governments of other countries participating in the Economic Conference to agree to the tariff standstill. This resolution not only mentions tariffs, but also involves import quotas and other plans to restrict trade. As for the existing policies of various countries, they can still be carried out freely. Therefore, the United Kingdom can continue its commercial treaty negotiations. It is found that the Organizing Committee is composed of representatives from eight countries, namely the United Kingdom, France, Germany, Belgium, the United States, Italy, Japan, and Norway. According to the resolution passed today, the Organizing Committee advises other countries to agree not to increase or create difficulties that hinder international trade before June 12 or at the time of the meeting. (12th Reuters Telegram)

Brussels Today, the Belgian cabinet has obtained the same financial and monetary dictatorial powers as the US government. Before the summer recess, the lower house of Congress granted the government the power to reduce political expenses, change official salaries, amend taxes, tariffs, and raise domestic and foreign debts by a vote of ninety-six to eighty-two, and can also take measures to curb economic behavior that hinders national credit when necessary. It is generally believed that this provision gives the government the power to deal with attacks on the franc. When the US dollar fluctuated greatly, the Belgian franc was in danger of being encircled and forced to depreciate. Therefore, the Belgian Prime Minister, in view of the storms encountered by the United States and the depreciation of the US dollar, believes that the government needs to obtain this power and stated that it will severely deal with any attempts to manipulate the foreign exchange market and suppress the franc domestically, and will also use this power to fully cooperate with such attempts abroad. (12th National Telegram)

Argentine Capital Tonight, the President of Argentina declared that the Argentine government is prepared to sign a reciprocal commercial treaty with the United States, and it is expected that this draft treaty can be negotiated within a few days. After the signing of this treaty, it will be the first result produced by the Washington secret economic talks. Argentina has sent a special envoy to cooperate with the ambassador to the United States to discuss the agenda of the World Economic Conference and the possibility of concluding a trade agreement with the US President. Since the United States imposed high protection taxes, Argentina's products have become increasingly narrow in the United States. When other countries followed suit to build similar barriers, Argentina's business was hit even harder, so it is urgently seeking to negotiate special measures for intra-American trade with neighboring countries. Therefore, it first negotiated a reciprocal agreement with the United States, and at the same time negotiated a commercial treaty with the United Kingdom, but it is believed that the items listed in the two treaties may not be the same. (12th National Telegram)

(Washington) The US President today signed the Rural Relief Act, which is attached with the privilege of inflating currency, but since the President has no intention of immediately exercising this power, it is generally expected that the inflation currency will be released at least after the World Economic Conference is closed, because the economic truce of the world will depend on the rational stability of exchange rates. (Tokyo) Soviet Russian Ambassador to Japan Yurenev visited Foreign Minister Uchida this afternoon to urge the Japanese government to decide on the issue of the transfer of the Eastern Railway. The reasons why Soviet Russia is eager to decide on the issue are obviously as follows: Since the establishment of "Manchukuo" and the completion of the railway, the Eastern Railway has lost its military and economic value. If the Eastern Railway continues to be jointly operated, it will leave the root of disputes between Japan, Manchuria, and Russia forever. If the Eastern Railway is transferred to Japan, which has financial resources, in addition to preventing future diplomatic disputes, it will also be easy to implement the five-year plan. As for the payment method of the sale price, in addition to the annual payment from the profit and cash of the Eastern Railway, part of it will be paid in kind, or the government of the buying country will be used as a loan to Russia. Therefore, when Ambassador Ota and Foreign Minister Litvinov met in Moscow on the 2nd, they stated that the sale of the Eastern Railway would formally recognize "Manchukuo", because the Soviet Union's disapproval resolution of the League of Nations has no relationship, so there is no hindrance. On the Issue of Real Strength in Disarmament, Germany Will Ultimately Be Forced to Yield

Hitler Schedules Opening of Reichstag

Neurath Visits Hindenburg

▲Reuters, Geneva, 12th The compromise proposal of the chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, will demonstrate the scope of Germany's demands to the world, including absolute equality in armaments and the inclusion of French reservists in the total number of deployable troops. It is reported that the United States will raise serious questions about Germany's demands in Berlin today. It is also reported that Germany is now showing a strong tendency to yield on the issue of real strength. German representative Nadolny said when leaving the meeting this afternoon, "The overall situation has now cleared away the thorns, and we can move forward."

▲Reuters, Washington, 13th President Roosevelt and Schacht, President of the Reichsbank, issued a joint statement saying that the World Economic Conference cannot succeed without disarmament. Schacht is a representative of the German government and is currently in Washington meeting with President Roosevelt and others to discuss economic matters.

▲Reuters, Berlin, 13th The German cabinet has decided to convene the Reichstag next Wednesday to hear German Chancellor Hitler's remarks on the situation of the Disarmament Conference. It is reported that Hitler will explain Germany's attitude towards disarmament and deny responsibility for the failure of the Disarmament Conference. The government's announcement of the convening of the Reichstag has attracted great attention in political circles, as it is known that if the Disarmament Conference fails, Germany will face a serious decision, namely, whether to declare the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles invalid based on other countries' refusal to disarm. German Foreign Minister Neurath visited President Hindenburg yesterday afternoon to report on the international political situation. Social Democratic members can attend the Reichstag session. The German government has chosen the Reichstag as the venue for its speech because it can attract greater attention than in Geneva. It is reported that the German Chancellor will also respond to the recent remarks made by British Secretary of State for War Hailsham in the House of Lords. The Germans believe that Hailsham's attacks are more severe than others, so the German government can no longer remain silent.

▲Havas, Washington, 12th The President of the German Central Bank, Schacht, discussed the arms issue with President Roosevelt. Roosevelt explained the US government's views on the matter, saying that the maintenance of peace in Europe depends on the attitude of the United States and Germany. The United States' recognition of participation in the International Consultation Treaty means that the sacrifices made in abandoning traditional diplomatic issues are not small. This consultation treaty is not only beneficial to France, Britain, Belgium, Poland, and the Little Entente countries, but also beneficial to Germany. Germany should also make some sacrifices to ensure the success of the Disarmament Conference. What we hope from Germany is: (1) gradually reduce the national defense force; (2) do not demand the establishment of offensive weapons that Germany does not currently have. Roosevelt further stated that if Germany can change its views, France will agree to gradually reduce offensive weapons. If this is done, in five years, countries will make significant progress on the path of universal disarmament. Roosevelt also urged the German government to consider the situation. Schacht did not agree with Roosevelt's words very much, but promised to report to Chancellor Hitler. This is why Schacht postponed his return to his country.

▲Guomin, Geneva, 12th This afternoon, Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson visited German representative Nadolny and agreed that Henderson should suggest to other national representatives that the General Committee should meet on Sunday to discuss Sections 1 and 2 of Part 2 of the British plan, namely, those concerning military strength, war materials, and armaments. This proposal has been accepted by Germany. If the General Committee can adopt it on Sunday, procedural disputes can be eliminated. However, there are still many difficulties in the form and strength of the armies of European countries, as well as their war preparations, which need to be resolved. It is reported that US representative Davis is currently in London working on a compromise plan based on Germany's right to equal treatment.

▲Havas, Geneva, 13th German representative to the Disarmament Conference, Nadolny, declared that he would leave Geneva this afternoon and return to Geneva next Friday after Chancellor Hitler made a declaration on foreign policy in the Reichstag. The Disarmament Conference is now planning to begin a major debate. The holding of this debate was decided by the Presidium of the Disarmament Conference and with Germany's consent. Although Rheinbaben is acting as the German chief representative in the absence of the German chief representative, it is questionable whether this debate can be as effective as expected. Events in Geneva and Berlin next Sunday will have great significance from an international perspective, which is generally recognized.

▲Havas, London, 13th US Chief Delegate to the Disarmament Conference, Davis, left London for Geneva at 2 PM this afternoon.

Quarantine Station Established in Manzhouli

(Harbin) Information received here today indicates that there is an outbreak of typhoid fever in Chita. It has been spreading since March, and now the spread is widening. A quarantine station has been established in Manzhouli to prevent the epidemic from spreading into Manchuria. Eastern Siberia, including Vladivostok, has now been infected with the disease. According to reliable estimates, no less than 10,000 men, women, and children have died from the epidemic. (13th, Reuters Telegram)

Austrians Hostile to Germans

▲Guomin, Vienna, 12th In view of the imminent visit of German government officials and National Socialist Party leaders to Austria, the Austrian government, through its police authorities, has promulgated several rules to ensure that German tourists experience various inconveniences. The Berlin Local Gazette believes that these new rules are hostile to German government officials and says that these regulations are even stricter than the treatment of tourists from enemy countries visiting Austria. For example, the number of people welcoming German guests at the airfield must not exceed twenty, German guests must not make any political speeches, the number of cars accompanying German guests touring Vienna must not exceed ten, and the police should disperse idlers gathering to watch German guests parading through the city. All of these are impolite expressions towards the government of a friendly nation. Furthermore, two of the three gatherings originally planned by Austrian groups during the visit of German dignitaries have now been banned, and the third is limited to its announced purpose, which is to commemorate the 250th anniversary of the relief of Vienna after being besieged by the Turks. However, if the scope of the meeting is temporarily not adhered to, speakers will be prohibited from speaking, and the audience will be dispersed.

Gandhi's Hunger Strike Situation

▲Reuters, Pune, 13th Gandhi began fasting on the 8th and is now as lucid as ever, but he is unable to move without assistance, and he cannot even raise his hand to shake his spinning wheel. Many of his most loyal followers are now gathered around him, including the famous poet and orator Mrs. Naidu, and they are all very worried. Gandhi also fasted last September to advocate for the untouchables, intending to die if necessary. After a week, he resumed eating due to a negotiated plan to improve the status of the untouchables.

Tianjin Telegram To Shen Bao, Regarding your newspaper's report on the 10th of this month that our company suffered another bombing incident on the 6th, this is a rumor spread by a Japanese newspaper. We have ordered a correction. Please correct the error. Thank you. Ta Kung Pao Yuan.

The Enemy Army Launches a General Offensive on All Our Routes (Dada)

Intense Fighting on All Routes in Luandong and Gubeikou

Special dispatch from Beiping, the Japanese army, disregarding world condemnation, has massively invaded Shanhaiguan, plotting to occupy Beiping and Tianjin and complete their North China conspiracy. In recent days, they have actively advanced, and the troops invading Luandong are attempting to cross the Luan River and advance westward. At the same time, large forces have been added to each pass of the Great Wall and launched a general offensive against us today (11th). Their brutal aircraft arbitrarily drop heavy, highly explosive bombs in various cities outside our undefended war zones, disregarding humanity and harming innocent civilians. This morning (11th), planes even arrived in Beiping to scout and disseminate absurd and inflammatory leaflets to pave the way for the invasion of Beiping and Tianjin. Their absolute ambition can be said to be completely exposed at this point, and their mask of deceiving the world is almost completely torn off. The situation in various directions is recorded as follows:

Combat Situation on Each Invading Route

After the Japanese army in Luandong launched a general offensive against us, they divided their forces to invade Funing, Qian'an, Lulong, and Changli. Only a small number of our troops were stationed in Luandong to maintain local security and railway transportation. There were no large armies defending it at first. After the Japanese army successively captured Funing, Qian'an, and Lulong, they planned to attack Changli and further planned to cross the river and advance westward. Our army, according to a predetermined plan, successively concentrated on the original positions on the west bank of the Luan River, defending the river. Only a small number of cavalry were left east of the Luan River for警戒. Yesterday, the Japanese and puppet troops that invaded Lulong pressed towards our Weng Division on the east bank of the Luan River on one side and attacked Changli from the side on the other. Our Changli cavalry was surrounded by the enemy, and after a courageous resistance, they finally broke through. Last night, enemy troops were discovered in Anshan Town, west of Changli, and Anshan Station was also shelled. In order to protect its flanks and consolidate the front, our army's alert troops and armored vehicles withdrew to Shimen Station on the east bank of the Luan River. Today, the Japanese army is still advancing west along the Pingyu Road. Our cavalry on the Beining Line is still fighting the enemy. If necessary, they will retreat across the Luan River Bridge to hold fast to the river. Enemy troops on the upper reaches of the Luan River are currently preparing to advance westward from Qian'an and Lulong and cross the Luan River. Yesterday, a unit of Japanese infantry, under the cover of intense artillery fire, attempted to cross the river and was repelled by our army. Our units in western Luandong have effectively coordinated to prevent the enemy from advancing westward. This morning, fierce fighting is taking place near Shimen, and on the banks of the river in Qian'an and Lulong. The Japanese army's invasion of Luandong this time includes three brigades in addition to the puppet army. Yesterday, two more brigades were transported from Dalian to Qinhuangdao. These two brigades are fresh troops newly transferred from Japan. The Fengshan Road is full of military vehicles, and the transportation of military supplies is very busy. Judging from the situation, they will not stop until they cross the river in a large-scale westward invasion to disturb Beiping and Tianjin. In the Gubeikou area, the enemy recently added a brigade and began to move from the day before yesterday, launching a general offensive against us today (11th). Yesterday evening, the enemy at Nantianmen shelled us fiercely. At 7 PM, two battalions of infantry attacked our positions in Daohuang Village, Yongquan Village, and other places. After three hours of fierce fighting, the enemy suffered heavy casualties and retreated to Nantianmen. Yongquan Village was bombed by the enemy with incendiary bombs, causing a fire that was quickly extinguished. In the Chetouyu area, about 400-500 infantry attacked yesterday afternoon at 6 PM and were repelled by one of our divisions. This morning (11th), the enemy launched a general offensive on all lines against our positions in Xinkailing, Daohuang Village, Shangdianzi, Chetouyu, and other places. The fighting is extremely fierce. As of the time of writing, the fighting is still going on. The enemy attaches great importance to Gubeikou and Xifengkou, preparing to launch a general offensive. Fierce fighting has already broken out in the Luowenyu area this morning, and fighting is also about to break out in other areas. The Japanese army attaches great importance to the Gubeikou and Xifengkou routes, intending to take advantage of this route to raid Beiping and Tianjin and threaten our entire front line in order to achieve its strategic goals quickly.

Fury of Soldiers at the Front

The large-scale invasion by the Japanese army was long expected by us. The authorities have had detailed consultations with Song Zheyuan, Shang Zhen, Pang Bingxun, Wan Fulin, He Zhuguo, and others in Beiping regarding the defense plan, and a general agreement has been reached. He Zhuguo returned to defense this morning, and Song, Pang, Shang, and others are also scheduled to go to the front tomorrow to make arrangements. The generals are indignant at the Japanese army's step-by-step advances, making our endurance impossible. Now that we have reached the final juncture, we are determined to fight to the death to defend our territory. Even if only one soldier remains, we will fight to the end. As for the soldiers at the front, they are particularly outraged by the Japanese army's tyranny, and they are sharpening their swords and waiting, preparing to kill the enemy. (11th)

A General Account of the War in Chahar (Continuation 1) (Special Correspondent Guo An)

(3) The Situation of the Past Week

The facts have proven that Liu Guitang and others, carrying the banner of Japanese imperialism, occupied Dolon. Following this, they actively moved troops and supplies of military equipment on the vast plains west of Rehe. Needless to say, the enemy's tense movements meant that the order for a general attack on Guyuan would soon be issued. However, although it seemed tense on the surface, in reality, it was only a thousand or so Japanese soldiers driving tens of thousands of our compatriots, those traitors who had lost their minds and souls, to serve as shock troops. At the same time, the enemy's actions this week seemed like a mixture of smoke screens and flares. Although the enemy was playing a bewildering game within the borders of Chahar Province, we can still determine that the Japanese army cannot use large forces. The maximum extent to which they are currently rampant in Chahar and Suiyuan is the puppet army, supplemented by some heavy firearms and advanced weapons such as tanks and airplanes. In any case, the main attacking force is being borne by the puppet army. It is obvious that on that desert-like plain, supplies and drinking water are very scarce, and the Japanese army's objective for the time being does not involve actively occupying Chahar and Suiyuan. Therefore, they are cunningly driving those heartless rebels to go and do it, not caring about their lives or deaths.

The first step of the enemy's plan to attack Chahar, the occupation of Dolon, has been completed. According to the current situation, the main force attacking Guyuan will certainly advance along the Zhangdu Road. It will not avoid the Zhangdu Road and advance west because there is no need for that kind of deep, long-range offensive strategy at the moment. Furthermore, an inner-line attack from Fengning towards Dushikou and Chicheng is also unlikely to happen for the time being because Sun's army is defending the Zhishanling area. If they abandon the plan to attack Guyuan from Dolon and implement an inner-line encirclement and attack, it will clearly result in another stalemate. Unless the troops attacking Guyuan are successful, the inner-line attack plan will commence. Not only will it threaten our troops defending Guyuan, but it will also give the right rear of Zhangjiakou a major blow. However, as the enemy advances south from the Duo-Zhang road, their right flank will inevitably be threatened by mixed cavalry units, forcing our army to retreat to the final defensive line. However, the enemy's attacks have not been fully prepared this week.

Since the enemy entered Dolon, the actions of the puppet rebel army have been completely like those of bandits. In some places, they are even worse than bandits. Therefore, the Japanese army also feels that it is somewhat difficult to command these rebellious and lawless fellows. Therefore, on the one hand, they are reorganizing the system of the rebel army, and on the other hand, they are mobilizing reinforcements. Although the telegrams advertise that the rebel army's advancing attack troops are demonstrating and harassing our army's positions, this action is entirely out of fear of our army's counterattack. Little do they know that those of our defending soldiers at the front are...................

From the time Dolon was lost until now, the area in front of Guyuan has been peaceful. We have gathered no less than 50,000 troops in the Guyuan and Zhangbei areas, with complete infantry, cavalry, and artillery units. Therefore, although the enemy believes that attacking Guyuan from the front is attacking our army's weak point, they cannot but be cautious. Moreover, there is the possibility of a renewed outbreak of the war in Luandong. In this way, the enemy's attempt to attack Chahar may have to be suspended for another three or two weeks. The difficulties that our army is currently experiencing are supplies and transportation equipment. At the same time, the biggest weakness is the lack of unified command. There are all kinds of troops. In name, everyone is united and helping each other, but in reality, everyone is looking out for themselves. Those who cannot fight well will run away first, and those who are slow to run will be unlucky. Wasn't that the case at the beginning of the war in Rehe? Kailu retreated to Chifeng, some surrendered and some ran away, and even those who did not run were scared away by him. The most worrying thing is the troops reorganized from the volunteer army. Although they have been fighting hard for two years and have combat experience, they lack ammunition replenishment and have not received any training. However, although we are worried about this, we also dare to believe that their willingness to sacrifice is great. (To be continued)

Japanese Aircraft Reconnoiters Beiping (Rate)

Circling Over the City of Beiping and Opening Fire with Machine Guns; Our Authorities Notify All Ambassadors to Protect Nationals

Special Dispatch from Beiping: The Japanese army, using our military's provocation as a pretext, is once again attacking Luandong. When Ayazawa came to China, he seemed to have intended to plot activities, so his movements were mysterious, probably carrying a mission. However, since our country's attitude was firm and people from all walks of life treated him with indifference, Ayazawa's cunning plan ultimately could not be implemented, and he left in disappointment. Recently, the attitude of the Japanese authorities has changed, and since various countries have remained silent on the recent battle of Rehe and the Great Wall, and the great powers have shown no sign of intervention to this day, the Japanese army's atrocities have become even more unscrupulous. In recent days, Luandong's Funing, Qian'an, Lulong, and Changli areas have fallen into enemy hands, and the situation has suddenly become tense. Its military actions are even more aggressive than the previous attack on Luandong. Heavy fighting has been taking place in the Gubeikou area since last night, with all Japanese troops launching a general offensive, clearly attempting to annex both Beiping and Tianjin. They are advancing step by step, and the situation is becoming increasingly dangerous. Yesterday, two Japanese planes flew successively to the eastern suburbs of Beiping, outside Chaoyangmen, Sunhe, and Guanyintang, to conduct reconnaissance. Because it was at night, it did not attract public attention. The local authorities received reports at that time and immediately increased vigilance. Air defense facilities had already been prepared, so they ordered all city air defense personnel to mobilize and calmly deploy. The order in the city center remained calm as usual. Today (11th), just after 5:00 AM, the sound of aircraft was suddenly heard again near Chaoyangmen. Two Japanese planes, entirely silver-gray, with the Rising Sun flag painted on their wings, flew from the northeast, passed Dongsi Pailou, and scattered leaflets there, then turned west and flew to Zhongnanhai, circling once above Jurentang, then passed Beihai and flew to Ganshiqiao, firing machine guns downward. At that time, the morning light had not yet risen, and residents in the city were still sound asleep. Only a few vegetable vendors were rushing to the market. The streetlights were still on, and there were few pedestrians. Moreover, the Japanese planes were flying at an altitude of more than 2,700 meters. Machine gun bullets fell from the sky, making sounds as they hit the roof tiles, but because of their weak force, they did not explode. Although eyewitnesses at the time fled in panic, no one was injured. The Japanese planes then flew south to Xidan Pailou, out of Xuanwumen, around Caishikou, and over Tianqiao, flying to Nanyuan, conducting reconnaissance for a long time. Finally, they flew north along the city walls via Zuo'anmen. They did not drop any bombs. After daybreak, rumors had spread throughout the city. There was no significant panic in the city. Many tourists still visited theaters, cinemas, and parks. However, some wealthy families sought refuge in the Legation Quarter or moved to the Tianjin Concession. The number of passengers going to Tianjin at the East Railway Station was more crowded than in the previous two days. When the Japanese planes flew to Beiping, the soldiers guarding Chaoyangmen fired several anti-aircraft guns. Anti-aircraft guns also traced the sky above Jurentang. The Japanese planes, knowing that we were prepared, left in a hurry. Currently, the embassies in the Legation Quarter are paying close attention to this matter and are inquiring with the Japanese Embassy about the truth. Our authorities have already notified all ambassadors to do their best to protect nationals of various countries in Beiping to ensure their safety. Most of the Japanese women and children in the eastern city have been ordered to leave Beiping a few days ago, heading to the Northeast or returning home. The true intentions of the Japanese army are already clear. Furthermore, various municipal schools in Beiping are quite concerned about the safety of the students due to the enemy planes coming to scout and scatter absurd leaflets this morning. Therefore, the principals of various elementary schools sent representatives to the Social Affairs Bureau of the Municipal Government at 11:00 AM today to petition for two things: (1) digging cellars in each school; (2) suspending classes every morning or seeking other appropriate measures. Secretary-General Wu Mangong of the Social Affairs Bureau received them and decided to take responsibility for planning the safety of the students. The cost of digging cellars will be estimated by each school and submitted to the bureau for approval. The issue of suspending classes will be answered after a decision is made with the bureau chief. The representatives left at about 12:00 noon and are actively planning. It is said that various universities in Beiping are also considering starting summer vacation early. (May 11)

Another Civil War Erupts in Sichuan

The 24th and 28th Armies Clash in Chongqing; the War Zone Spreads, and the Situation Gradually Escalates

Dispatch from Chongqing: Sichuan warlords Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui, due to conflicts of interest, disregarding everything at a time of national crisis, launched a civil war. After more than three months of fighting, they finally announced the end and temporarily returned to calm. Who knew that the 24th and 28th armies would openly start fighting again on the 5th of this month? The 29th Army has also been drawn into the vortex, and the situation is gradually escalating, with the possibility of affecting the overall situation. The Guizhou war is currently in full swing, and the Sichuan war has started again. Half of the southwest is without a single piece of clean land. The reasons for the re-eruption of the Sichuan war and the recent war situation are summarized below:

Long-Term Causes of the Re-Eruption of the Sichuan War

In the previous Sichuan war, the 24th Army designated Wenhui as the target of public criticism, and was besieged by all parties. However, Liu had very flexible skills, and had the power to disintegrate the allied forces. As a result, all parties were still unmoved. Only the 28th Army, under Deng Xihou, feigned cooperation with Liu. In order to save the army from danger and relieve the encirclement, Liu Wenhui instigated all the army's generals to support Deng Xihou as the commander-in-chief of the army, directing military affairs on the front line, and promised to designate Shuangliu and Chongqing counties as Deng's defense area, and also assisted Deng's army with 5 million yuan. However, later, as the war became tight and the 24th Army's front line was in danger, Deng Xihou actually confiscated all the military funds and defense areas, remained stationed and did not move. When Tian Songyao of the 29th Army launched a rebellion and street fighting broke out in Chengdu, the Huang Yimin division and other units of Deng's army sneaked into the 29th Army headquarters, secretly helping Tian's army attack Liu Wenhui, intending to eliminate the 24th Army and solve the problem fundamentally. However, Liu Wenhui, in extreme danger, boosted morale and defeated the 29th Army, driving Tian Songyao out of Chengdu. At this time, Deng Xihou came forward again to mediate, and the two sides ceased fighting and negotiated peace. As a result, the various units of the 29th Army concentrated and launched a counterattack in an unhurried manner, re-enacting street fighting in the provincial capital. The 28th Army not only did not help Liu Wenhui, or declared neutrality, but still sent troops to besiege the 24th Army. At that time, Liu Wenhui, the commander of the 24th Army, and all the generals of the army, hated Deng to the bone. However, because they were surrounded on all sides at the time, they did not dare to compete, and endured and waited for the time to raise an army to question the crime, so they left the root of the disaster for the re-eruption of the Sichuan war.

Main Forces of the Participating Armies

This Sichuan war is headed by Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army. Although the 24th Army lost more than half of its defense area after the previous war, its strength was not greatly damaged. After the reorganization of the entire army, there were a total of ten divisions, including the first division commander Zhang Zhihe, the second division commander Lin Yungeng, the third division commander Xia Shoukun, the fourth division commander Tang Yonghui, the fifth division commander Wang Yuanhu, the sixth division commander Chen Hongwen, the seventh division commander Leng Nanxun, the eighth division commander Qing Feiru, the ninth division commander Li Yushu, the tenth division commander Chen Nengfen, the first brigade commander Lai Mutian, the second brigade commander Kang Qiufan, the third brigade commander Huang Ao, the fourth brigade commander Huang Qixian, the fifth brigade commander Liu Wencai, the sixth brigade commander Liu Zhucun, the seventh brigade commander Kou Chengqing, the eighth brigade commander Liu Yuantang, the ninth brigade commander Wang Zhiren, the tenth brigade commander Lin Meipo, the eleventh brigade commander Yang Shangzhou, the twelfth brigade commander Fu Yuanxi, the thirteenth brigade commander Xu Guangpu, the fourteenth brigade commander Zhang Zhifang, the fifteenth brigade commander Yu Zhongying, the sixteenth brigade commander Peng Chengfu, the seventeenth brigade commander Yu Songlin, the eighteenth brigade commander Zhao Peisan, the nineteenth brigade commander Shi Zhaowu, the twentieth brigade commander Mou Guangming, the twenty-first brigade commander Cheng Zimin, the twenty-second brigade commander Huang Xixuan, the twenty-third brigade commander Xiong Cihou, the twenty-fourth brigade commander Gao Binzong, the twenty-fifth brigade commander Su Huazhou, the twenty-sixth brigade commander Duan Kerui, the twenty-seventh brigade commander Zhu Yinzhou, the twenty-eighth brigade commander Yang Zongli, the twenty-ninth brigade commander Chen Ruiting, and the thirtieth brigade commander Mou Suifang. Each division has 10,000 people, totaling 100,000 troops. The defense areas include Huayang, Chongqing, Xinjin, Shuangliu, Qiongzhou, Pujiang, Dayi, Meishan, Pengshan, Danling, Qingshen, Ya'an, Tianquan, Mingshan, Lushan, Rongjing, Hanyuan, Jixing, Jiading, Jiajiang, Hongya, Jianwei, Leibo, Mabian, Emei, Xichang, Mianning, Yuexun, Huili, Yanyuan, Yanbian, Zhaojue, and even 14 counties in Xikang, a total of 47 counties. The 28th Army, under Deng Xihou, which is standing against the 24th Army, did not suffer any major losses in the previous Sichuan war, and instead increased in number, totaling five divisions, including the first division commander Chen Shunong, the second division commander Huang Yin, the third division commander Ma Dezai, the teaching division commander Yang Rongbai, the model division commander Chen Jingshan, the first brigade commander You Guangju, the second brigade commander Wang Xuejiang, the third brigade commander Sun Gongsong, the fourth brigade commander Wang Shijun, the fifth brigade commander Diao Wenjun, the sixth brigade commander Liu Gaohuai, the seventh brigade commander Luo Naifan, the eighth brigade commander Zhou Shiying, the ninth brigade commander Liu Naizhu, the tenth brigade commander Xie Dekan, the eleventh brigade commander Rao Guangyu, the twelfth brigade commander Li Shuhua, the thirteenth brigade commander Gong Weiqing, the fourteenth brigade commander Liu Danwu, and the fifteenth brigade commander Niu Xiguang. Each division has 12,000 people, totaling 60,000 people. The defense areas include Wenjiang, Pixian, Chongning, Guanxian, Xinfan, Guanghan, Xindu, Jintang, Songpan, Lifan, Maogong, Maozhou, Wenchuan, Pengxian, and even three counties in Gansu, totaling 17 counties. As for the 29th Army, under Tian Songyao, which is fully engaged in suppressing bandits in northwestern Sichuan, now that Bazhong, Tongjiang, and Nanjiang have been successively recovered, in addition to handling the aftermath, the entire army has concentrated in Chengdu, preparing to participate in the re-eruption of the Sichuan war, jointly fighting the 24th Army with the 28th Army.

Immediate Causes of the Re-Eruption of the Sichuan War

Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army, having suffered significant impact from Deng Xihou in the previous Sichuan war, thought of revenge every day, but had no excuse to use. Previously, Chen Shunong, the commander of the third division of the Sichuan-Kang Army, who was under Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army, received 160,000 yuan from Liu every month to maintain the status quo. When the war broke out, Chen Shunong refused to accept Liu Wenhui's orders, remained stationed and did not move, and took the opportunity to seize territory, and publicly declared his separation from the 24th Army and returned to the established system, still under the command of Deng Xihou. Liu Wenhui then used this as an excuse to ask Deng to compensate for the military funds that Chen Shunong had been receiving, and demanded that Chen cede the two counties of Jianyang and Lezhi where he lived, otherwise he would resolve the issue by force. Deng Xihou has always been able to endure humiliation and make concessions to all parties. This time, he uniquely considered Liu's request unreasonable and refused sternly. He also actively engaged in military preparations. Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army then convened a meeting of all army generals to discuss practical solutions. As a result, they all advocated using force against Deng to determine the outcome. Thus, on the 5th of this month, the 5th division commander Wang Yuanhu of the 24th Army and the 2nd division commander Huang Yin of the 28th Army engaged in a direct confrontation in Shiyangchang, Chongqing County. Thus, the Sichuan situation, which had just returned to calm, was disturbed and underwent a major change.

Recent Battlefield Situation Between the Two Armies

At the beginning of this Sichuan war, the fighting was limited to within the territory of Chongqing County. There was no movement elsewhere. And the military actions of the two armies in Chongqing County once stopped. The generals of the 24th and 28th armies, who belonged to the Baoding faction, were running around calling for peace and eliminating the civil war. However, both sides insisted on their original purpose and refused to make concessions. On the morning of the 4th, Deng Xihou of the 28th Army openly left the province for Jianyang to deploy military affairs. By the 7th, major battles had broken out between the 24th and 28th armies in Chongqing and Wenjiang, as well as in Jianyang and Renshou. In the end, due to the large number of troops in the 24th Army, superior equipment, and a hundredfold momentum, the 28th Army, outnumbered, announced its retreat. On the 8th, Wang Yuanhu's unit of the 20th Army occupied Wenjiang of the 28th Army. The 24th Army in Renshou also approached Jianyang. Wherever the vanguard went, the 28th Army had no combat capability and collapsed immediately. Deng Xihou was quite panicked. He has now completely concentrated the troops stationed in various garrison areas in Chengdu, Pixian, Guanxian, Jianyang, and other places, preparing to fight the 25th Army to the death. At the same time, he telegraphed and urged Tian Songyao of the 29th Army to quickly send troops to help. Tian has replied and allowed the deployment of three divisions to help. The Zeng Xianlian division has been dispatched to Jianyang, and Wang Mingzhang has been dispatched to Chengdu, ready to provide assistance as needed. The Sichuan war situation is about to expand.

70 Million People Call for Peace

The 70 million people of Sichuan have not yet recovered from the previous Sichuan war. The fierce flames of the Red bandits have not stopped causing disturbances. Having survived the disaster, how can they endure another war? When the 24th and 28th armies engaged in a direct confrontation, all parties actively ran around, calling for peace, eliminating the civil war, and jointly resisting foreign aggression. However, the warlords are brave in private fights and do not consider all parties at all, acting willfully, which has aroused public anger. The Great Alliance against Warlord Civil War has been established in Chengdu and Chongqing. Sub-alliances have also been established in various counties, standing on the united front, opposing warlord civil war, resisting donations and taxes, and stopping the supply of military funds, in order to avoid the expansion of the incident. The 70 million people of Sichuan have sent a telegram to the two army commanders Deng and Liu, requesting them to immediately stop military actions, so as not to become public enemies of the Sichuan people and be abandoned by the people of the country. The original telegram read: "To Army Commander Liu of Chengdu, Zigan, and please forward to Army Commander Deng, Jinkang: According to reports, the troops of the two armies have started a civil war in Chongqing Prefecture and have spread to Wenjian, Piguan, and other places, with a tendency to expand. The entire peaceful Sichuan situation has been plunged into a continuous state of war, and the sufferers are our people. As we are currently in a time of serious national crisis, with North China in danger, the Japanese invaders are bound to advance. The Red flames in Jiangxi, Hubei, and Zhejiang are in full swing. All soldiers should concentrate their military strength to resist foreign aggression and appease the country, to fulfill their duties in one in ten thousand ways, and should not launch civil wars, shake the foundations of the country, and leave behind mockery for foreign countries. The two of you are military leaders and pillars of the Party and the country, so we do not hesitate to earnestly persuade you, hoping to arouse your conscience, immediately stop military actions, and jointly maintain the peace of Sichuan. The people will rejoice like drinking sweet dew. A change of mind can achieve this. It is time to rein in at the edge of the cliff. The two of you are wise and should not abandon yourselves to the people of the country and isolate yourselves from the people, becoming public enemies of the 70 million people. The telegram is urgent, and we await your instructions. Sincerely, the 70 million people of Sichuan." (May 11)

The Water Police Headquarters Deploys Defense of the Yangtze River

The Directors of the Seven Provincial Branches Are Fully Appointed; the Navy Department Allocates Eight Warships to be Received Successively

Dispatch from Hankou: The Water Police Headquarters of the Yangtze River provinces has been established for a long time. Director Jiang Dingwen has also officially taken office. The deployment for the defense of the Yangtze River is extremely strict. The details are as follows:

Appointment of Directors of Each Branch

The provinces under the jurisdiction of the headquarters, from Sichuan, passing through Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, to Jiangsu and Zhejiang, total seven provinces. Branches are set up in each province. Some are reorganized from the Water Police Bureau, and some are recently established. The candidates for the branch directors have been carefully selected. It was not until yesterday (11th) that they were fully appointed. They are: He Beiheng, director of the Sichuan Branch; Xie Liangyu, director of the Hunan Branch; Zhang Ji, director of the Hubei Branch; Li Richeng, director of the Jiangxi Branch; Jiang Yi, director of the Anhui Branch; Shen Baoyi, director of the Jiangsu Branch; Zhejiang has two branches: Ouyang Ge, director of the first branch, managing the outer sea, and Liu Zhihou, director of the second branch, managing the inland river. A temporary maritime patrol team is also set up, with Zhu Songzhou as the team leader.

Receiving Naval Warships

The headquarters is responsible for the defense of the river, and the area is vast. In addition to the original gunboats of each province, which are completely under its jurisdiction, Chiang Kai-shek, chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, has ordered the Navy Department to allocate ten warships for its command and dispatch. The Navy Department, due to insufficient allocation, has temporarily allocated eight ships. Six ships, including Weisheng, Desheng, Guangyun, Hai'ou, Hai'ou, and Lie Ning fish boats, have arrived in Hankou and have been successively received by the headquarters, and water police flags have been added. The Chenzi and Zhangzi boats have not yet arrived in Hankou. Director Jiang Dingwen has ordered the Weisheng and Desheng boats to patrol Changsha. The remaining boats are stationed in various ports upstream and downstream to carry out patrols.

Drafting the Yangtze River Defense Plan

Director Jiang Dingwen has recently drafted a complete plan for the river defense of each province, which is extremely detailed. Yesterday, he specifically visited Director He Chengjun to discuss for a long time, exchange views, and planned to call the directors of each provincial branch and the captains of each boat to Hankou in the short term to hold a Yangtze River defense meeting to personally give instructions. Also, due to the lack of water police personnel, it was decided to set up a water police training school, which has been submitted to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for approval. The number of students, the length of the course, the subjects, and the budget are all in the plan. As soon as it is determined, the recruitment of water police students will begin, and training will be carried out. (May 12)

Amateur Sports Games of the People of Jiangyin

The county stadium held a two-day amateur sports game for the people starting today (13th). A total of 147 athletes from various people's education centers participated. The opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM today. County Magistrate Jin sent representative Secretary Han Yuansheng to preside over the ceremony. The sports activities started at 1:00 PM in the afternoon. In addition to track and field, ball games, and all-around sports, there were also tug-of-war, 200-meter pole carrying finals, free bike slow race finals, 50-meter literacy finals, and national skills. It ended at 5:00 PM. There are also competitions in the morning and afternoon tomorrow.

Changshu Police Officer Commits Suicide by Shooting

The 7th District Weijiatang is stationed with two squads of police. On the 12th of this month, there was a celebration for welcoming the gods. All the police officers in the team went out to maintain order. Only one sentry and Wu Huanzao, who was sick, were left in the team. Unexpectedly, at about 3:00 PM, the police officer on duty at the gate suddenly heard a gunshot from inside. He went in to check but found no one. Then he went to Wu's sickbed and saw bloodstains on his chest, a gun lying upside down in the corner of the bed. Wu had died. He rushed to report to the squad leader and others who returned. They then reported to the headquarters in the city, and Chief Wang reported to the county government, which sent an inspector to the countryside to inspect. The inspection found that Wu Huanzao had bullet holes in his chest and back. The bullet entered from the chest and came out of the back. It was indeed suicide. The team then sent someone to take care of the burial and notified the family to come to Changshu to collect the coffin.

A Large Number of Bandits Are Arrested in Hupu

Hupu in this county is located on the riverbank, and bandits can easily sneak in. Recently, because the fish season has arrived, many people from other places have come to the town. Yang Kun, the director of the local public security sub-bureau, was still worried that bandits might be mixed in, so he joined forces with Tang Yingxi, the company commander of the provincial security team stationed in the town, and others to carry out a large search starting on the 10th. Xia Delin and 23 others were arrested in the Dongtangxi area. According to the townspeople's guarantee, 17 of them were released on bail and deported. Xu Nanda, Xia Delin, Dong Jingshan, Yao Liangsheng, Sun Jisheng, and others were indeed identified as bandits and were escorted to the city on the 12th.

Investigation of the Excavation of Ancient Tombs in Suzhou

In the Xietang township of Wu County, there is an ancient tomb of Zhang Shicheng, the King of Gusu at the end of the Yuan Dynasty and the beginning of the Ming Dynasty. It is said that there are many funerary objects in the tomb. Recently, Mao Jinhe, a local tyrant in the township, hired many stonemasons and secretly excavated the tomb. Zou Xiaogong, the magistrate of Wu County, learned about this and believed that the tomb has a history of more than 500 years and should not be excavated. He ordered the Xietang District Office yesterday (13th) to strictly stop it, investigate the excavation situation, and report in detail for review.

Sheng's Lingering Garden to Be Opened as a Park

Sheng's Lingering Garden on Wufu Road has been managed by the county government since Sheng's property was sealed up. It has now been ordered to be returned. After Magistrate Zou contacted Sheng's representatives, it was decided that the garden would be returned to Sheng's on the 18th of this month. It is also learned that local people here have sent a letter to Sheng's, requesting that the Lingering Garden be opened as a park. Sheng's is currently considering this matter and it may become a reality.

Wuxi Scouts Begin Large-Scale Camping

The county-wide scout review and large-scale camping began on the 12th. At 2:00 PM, the schools took the lead with their blue team flags and slogans, departing from the schools. Those with baggage traveled by ox cart. Hundreds of athletes marched with great spirit all the way. When they arrived at the campsite under Baoshan Bridge in Huishan, they set up white tents, dug pits and buried pots, carried water and washed, and erected camp gates. The work was extremely busy. The schools that reported to the campsite included the county junior high school, the provincial junior high school attached elementary school, the Hu's junior high school, the civil vocational school, the Tonghuijiao elementary school, the Guangqin elementary school 2, the county party headquarters, and others. Those participating from other places included Changshu County Junior High School and Shimei Elementary School, a total of 47 schools. The camp facilities included a wireless radio, alarm bells, electric lights, a general camp, and a camp public security bureau, a rescue team, a news agency, and a store. The headquarters was set up in Huishan Park, with a bicycle communication team to transmit news. The organization was extremely meticulous. At about 8:00 PM that evening, a group leader talk was held. Yesterday (13th) morning, a scout rule story speech contest and course competition were held. The afternoon was a preparation review, and the evening was an anti-Japanese national salvation speech contest. The 14th was a morning course competition, a morning review ceremony, an afternoon course competition, and a camp station conference in the evening. On the morning of the 15th, there was a memorial week for the Prime Minister, a course performance, and an opening ceremony in the afternoon. The camp was broken at 6:00. Many trophies such as silver spires, silver shields, and silk flags were awarded by various agencies, groups, and newspapers. Zhang Zhongren, director of the preparatory committee of the China Boy Scout General Association, and Secretary Wang of the Ministry of Railways, came to Wuxi the night before to visit. Sun Yuanliang, commander of the 88th Division of the National Army, also arrived by train from the Danyang defense area last night for the review.

The Responsibility for the Purchase of Defective Weapons in Nantong is Clear

The self-defense weapons purchased in Nantong, including 40 submachine guns, were reported by Wu Jianzhang, a member of the county executive and supervisory committee, as being made of scrap materials. The newly appointed county magistrate, Ye Zhendong, verified that they were indeed useless and defective. All sectors of the local community were shocked. County Magistrate Ye noted that the handover file only had a note for 18,000 yuan issued by the former county magistrate Zhang Su, with no receipts. He sent a letter to Zhang on the 12th, requesting a detailed reply on the inside story of the case.

Issuance of Special Defense Donation Loan Certificates

The County Defense Council, because the income from defense donations was too slow, requested a resolution from the County Council to issue 40,000 yuan of special defense donation loan certificates on June 1. The certificate holders were allowed to cash out at a 97% discount. The certificates were divided into 50 yuan, 10 yuan, and 5 yuan denominations. In March of next year, they will be cashed out at full face value.

Hangzhou and Zhejiang Province Have Excellent Silkworm Crops

The Zhejiang Construction Department designated Xiaoshan and Lin'an counties as model silkworm mulberry areas for improving silk. A disturbance occurred earlier this month due to a misunderstanding among the villagers. The matter was properly handled and quickly subsided. It is now learned that the first model area in Xiaoshan sold 130,000 sheets of improved silkworm eggs this year. Most of the silkworms are now in their fourth instar. The silkworm crops are excellent. It is estimated that cocoons will be harvested around the 25th of this month. It is estimated that the entire area will harvest 27,000 piculs of fresh cocoons. In addition, the second model area in Lin'an sold more than 7,000 sheets of improved silkworm eggs. The silkworms are currently in their third instar. The cocoons will be harvested by the end of this month. If the weather does not change much, it is estimated that more than 18,000 piculs of fresh cocoons will be harvested. The silkworm crops in the improved areas of Hangxian, Haining, Jiaxing, and Haiyan are also excellent. The cocoon merchants in various counties are preparing to open the market.

Local News

Overseas Chinese Expelled from Mexico Telegraph for Relief

Distressed Overseas Chinese Telegraph Government Authorities Separately Yesterday

Municipal Government Also Sends Letter to Charitable Organizations Yesterday

Anti-Chinese sentiment in Mexico intensifies, with the situation becoming increasingly severe. The properties of all overseas Chinese in Mexico have been confiscated, and they have been expelled from the country. Consequently, batches of distressed overseas Chinese have returned to China, with four groups already arrived. These distressed individuals possess nothing but the clothes on their backs, presenting a pitiful sight. It is learned that the representatives of these distressed overseas Chinese, Huang Zhulin, Lin Wenli, Lin Huiyao, and others, telegraphed Chairman Lin, Chairman Chiang, and President Sun yesterday, seeking relief. The original telegrams are as follows:

Telegram to Chairman Lin

To Chairman Lin of the National Government in Nanjing,

Overseas Chinese in Mexico have suffered severe discrimination and been forced to return to China successively, penniless and in dire need of relief. Representatives have arrived in Shanghai on this day and urgently telegraph, earnestly requesting that you consider the sacrifices made by overseas Chinese for the country. Please promptly allocate a substantial sum from the Ministry of Finance to be distributed by the Shanghai Global Overseas Chinese General Association for immediate relief, addressing the immediate crisis. Furthermore, please carefully devise concrete measures to address the root cause. An urgent telegram, awaiting good news. Respectfully, representatives of distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico: Huang Zhulin, Lin Wenli, Lin Huiyao, et al. [“Wen” (文) follows names, typically used as a respectful closing]

Telegram to Chairman Chiang

To Chairman Chiang in Nanchang,

Anti-Chinese sentiment in Mexico forces our fellow countrymen to successively flee to the homeland. The situation is utterly miserable, lacking food and clothing, and in desperate need of relief. Representatives arrived in Shanghai on this day and urgently telegraph, earnestly requesting a substantial donation to be entrusted to the Shanghai Global Overseas Chinese General Association for distribution. An urgent telegram, awaiting good news. Respectfully, representatives of distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico: Huang Zhulin, Lin Wenyu, Lin Huiyao, et al. [“Wen” (文) follows names, typically used as a respectful closing]

Telegram to President Sun

To President Sun, care of the Central Daily News in Nanjing,

Distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico are successively returning home, urgently requiring relief. We urgently telegraph, earnestly requesting a substantial donation to be entrusted to the Shanghai Global Overseas Chinese General Association for distribution. Advance thanks and await your reply. Respectfully, representatives of distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico: Huang Zhulin, Lin Wenyu, Lin Huiyao, et al. [“Yuan Yin” (元印) follows names, unsure of exact meaning]

Municipal Government Letter

Letter from the Municipal Government to the China Northeast Refugees Relief Association, Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, Shanghai All Circles Relief Northeast Compatriots Association, Renji Hall, Xinwei Relief Association, Liaojihei Re Volunteer Army Support Association, Shanghai Local Association:

Respectfully,

Following the recent anti-Chinese surge in Mexico, overseas Chinese in Mexico have successively returned to China after much hardship. Upon investigation, these distressed overseas Chinese had all their properties confiscated by the Mexican government before their hasty departure, leaving them penniless and in a truly pitiful state. Previously, representatives of these distressed overseas Chinese, such as Li Kuan and others, reported to this government about their expulsion, and the situation of over two hundred distressed overseas Chinese awaiting assistance in Shanghai. This government has requested local organizations in this city to provide relief. Now, we have received another report that an additional forty-nine distressed overseas Chinese, including Lin Huiyao and others, urgently require assistance, making the situation quite pressing. We remember that these distressed overseas Chinese, while doing business overseas, have always generously contributed to disaster relief and resistance against foreign aggression within the country. They were, in the past, patriotic overseas Chinese. Now, due to expulsion, they are all victims who cannot return to their homes. Your esteemed association embraces their suffering and holds charity in your hearts. Recalling past contributions and emulating patriotism, please make every effort to provide relief to these overseas Chinese passing through Shanghai, enabling them to return to their respective hometowns. Your benevolence will spread far and wide and will be admired by overseas Chinese everywhere. We are sending this special letter and hope to receive a reply.

Conducting Investigation into Foreign Goods Dumping Situation

The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, recognizing that the dumping policy of foreign goods has greatly impacted China's industry and commerce, have established a Dumping Goods Review Committee to prevent this. Chu Minyi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Discussing Central Government Affairs and Borderland Situation

According to the Central News Agency, Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning and is scheduled to return to Nanjing by overnight train tonight. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Chu at his residence yesterday morning and inquired about the current situation in Xinjiang and various issues such as rural revitalization. He provided the following detailed answers:

Xinjiang is Calm According to Mr. Chu, the Xinjiang incident has now calmed down. The Xinjiang authorities previously dispatched Chen Zhong via Russia to Beijing to report on the current situation in Xinjiang and seek instructions on how to handle the situation. While traveling to Moscow, Chen learned that the central government had already formulated a plan for handling the Xinjiang incident and had appointed Huang Musong as the Pacification Commissioner to go to Xinjiang to offer condolences. Chen then returned to Xinjiang, conveying the intentions and plan of the central government to the people. The Hui people have always been obedient to the central government and decided to quietly await the arrival of Pacification Commissioner Huang to handle the situation. Pacification Commissioner Huang is scheduled to depart for Xinjiang next week. The group accompanying him consists of more than twenty people. It has not yet been decided whether they will fly to Xinjiang or travel via Siberia. As for the suggestion of the China Hui Culture Promotion Association to organize a new investigation committee, it seems feasible in order to resolve the Xinjiang incident as soon as possible.

Sichuan-Guizhou Internal Strife Liu Wenhui, Chairman of the Sichuan Provincial Government, has recently had a rift with Deng Xihou, commander of the Twenty-eighth Army. Wang Jialie, Chairman of the Guizhou Provincial Government, also has conflicts with You Guocai, commander of the Third Division stationed in Guizhou. Troops are currently being mobilized, and war clouds are gathering in Sichuan and Guizhou, with the potential for an imminent outbreak. At this time of serious national crisis, it is regrettable that internal strife is still occurring in Sichuan and Guizhou. The central government has sent separate telegrams to strictly stop the conflict and is awaiting the central government’s investigation and resolution.

Rural Revitalization Regarding the issue of revitalizing the rural economy, the Executive Yuan held a meeting in Beijing yesterday morning (the 12th) to discuss the outline of the implementation plan. In the future, it is planned to organize a specialized committee to study various issues such as improving agricultural implements and to establish associations in various provinces to be specifically responsible for implementation. The Executive Yuan will also hold daily meetings to discuss the issue of revitalizing the rural economy. As for the collateral for the Jiangsu-Zhejiang silk industry public bond, the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry are still in discussion and have not yet made a decision.

China Joins International Maritime Convention, Effective Today

Ministry of Communications Inspects and Improves Ship Equipment

According to the Kuomin News Agency, the International Convention for the Safety of Life at Sea was decided upon by the Ministry of Communications after consulting with the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Navy. China formally notified its accession as a member state on February 14 of this year. According to the provisions of the convention, accession becomes effective three months later and is to be strictly implemented. Three months have now passed, and it becomes effective today. In addition to notifying the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Navy to take note, the Ministry of Communications has also instructed navigation administrations in various regions to inform all shipping companies to pay attention. According to technical personnel from the Shanghai Navigation Administration, the convention was initiated in 1929, and the following nineteen countries have joined as member states: Germany, Austria, Belgium, Canada, Denmark, Spain, Ireland, China, England, the United States, France, Italy, Japan, Finland, Norway, Netherlands, Sweden, Soviet Russia, and India. The content generally focuses on the following five aspects: (1) ship structure, (2) life-saving equipment, (3) radio equipment, (4) navigation safety, and (5) ship certificates. Since joining, China has made special efforts to improve navigation ships and equip them perfectly to comply with the convention. The Ministry of Communications is currently inspecting and devising ways to proceed.

Ministry of Communications Sends Condolences to the Family of Schmidt of Eurasia Aviation Corporation

According to the Daily News Agency, after Schmidt, Director of Flight Operations of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, died in an accident during a flight in Germany, Li Jingcong, General Manager of the company, reported the details to the Ministry of Communications. Since Mr. Schmidt came to China, he has made significant contributions to the planning and assistance of postal aviation between Northwest China and Eurasia. At a time when Eurasia flights are being planned for connection, the sudden loss of such a talent is deeply regrettable. This telegram is sent to express our condolences and deepest sympathy.

Ministry of Communications

French Government Awards Medal to Qian Xinzhi

French Consul General Méléaud Represents Award

Qian Xinzhi, General Manager of the Four Banks Joint Treasury, has served as Vice Chairman of the Sino-French Bank for fifteen years. His planning and management have greatly benefited Sino-French trade and economy. In order to reward Qian Xinzhi for his service, the French government awarded him a medal. The medal arrived in Shanghai some days ago, and the award ceremony was held at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund at 1 p.m. yesterday. At the same time, a luncheon was held there, and Mayor Wu, Kong Xiangxi, Li Shizeng, and other important Chinese and foreign figures were invited to attend.

Guests Present

The important Chinese and foreign figures who were invited to attend and accompany the ceremony yesterday afternoon included: Mayor of Shanghai Wu Tiecheng, Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Central Supervisory Committee member Li Shizeng, Governor of the Central Bank Kong Xiangxi, Executive Yuan Secretary Chu Minyi, former League of Nations Secretary Wu Kaisheng, banking representatives Xu Xinliu, Li Fusun, Yu Zuoting, Zhou Zuomin, Wu Yunzhai; and from the French side, French Consul General Méléaud, Consul Delaquérière, Sino-French Bank Manager Barre, and other relevant foreigners, totaling more than thirty people.

Award Ceremony

The award ceremony was quite simple. After the Chinese and foreign guests arrived, champagne was first served. Then, at precisely 1 p.m., French Consul General Méléaud addressed the audience, saying, "The French government believes that Mr. Qian Xinzhi has made significant contributions to Sino-French economic cooperation, and therefore specifically instructs this Consul General to represent and award him a higher-level medal." After speaking, he presented the medal and pinned it on Qian's chest, and raised a glass to congratulate him. Then, Sino-French Bank Manager Barre delivered a congratulatory speech, and Qian's reply was translated by Liu Xichang, Secretary of the Sino-French Education Foundation. At 1:15 p.m., the ceremony was announced as complete. After the crowd raised their glasses once more to congratulate him, they proceeded to sit down for lunch. Guests and hosts enjoyed the banquet, which dispersed at 2:30 p.m.

Barre’s Speech

Sino-French Bank Manager Barre said in his speech, "Today, the Chinese guests participating in the award ceremony are all close friends of Mr. Qian Xinzhi. In addition, there are well-known French figures who have long been friendly to China who have also honored us with their presence. The French government has entrusted Consul Méléaud in Shanghai to present Mr. Qian Xinzhi with this medal of honor to express its admiration. I dare to believe that I can represent all of you in offering the most sincere congratulations to Mr. Qian Xinzhi. Our bank's Chairman Guo Ya Jun and General Manager Galé also sent telegrams entrusting me to congratulate Mr. Qian Xinzhi. I would like to take this opportunity to say to you that our bank's operations in China have a special situation. At the beginning of its establishment, the Chinese government sponsored this initiative and participated in the share capital. Therefore, there are also Chinese people on the board of directors. Mr. Qian Xinzhi is the Vice Chairman of our bank's board of directors and concurrently holds the position of Chinese General Manager, which shows the participation of China. In fact, it is Sino-French economic cooperation. In 1931, our bank in North China once implemented this kind of economic cooperation with major Chinese banks, but it was not important. Since then, there has been no action of any kind. The reason is the current worldwide economic panic. All banks have to engage in austerity and restrict lending. What we hope now is that this kind of economic panic will end soon, so that our bank can continue to carry out economic cooperation with major Chinese banks. Mr. Qian Xinzhi is a well-known figure in the Chinese financial community. He will be able to combine the Chinese banks and our bank, so that Sino-French economic cooperation can be implemented. Now, please raise your glasses to congratulate Mr. Qian."

Qian's Reply

Consul General and gentlemen, I am honored and extremely grateful to receive the medal from the French government through Consul General Méléaud. Please ask Consul General Méléaud to convey my gratitude to the French government. I am also deeply moved by Mr. Barre's compliments and praise, and I am also grateful for the congratulations entrusted by Chairman Guo Ya Jun and General Manager Galé. Please also ask Mr. Barre to convey my gratitude to Mr. Guo and Mr. Galé. Since the Chinese government assisted in the establishment of our bank, the inherent economic relationship between China and France has relied on the wisdom of Mr. Guo Ya Jun, Mr. Galé, Mr. Barre, and other famous figures, who have helped each other and allowed it to develop day by day. As for my personal aspect, the honorable President can firmly believe that I will do my best in the future to continue the Sino-French economic cooperation policy. This is my duty. Today I have this good opportunity to raise a glass with you all to wish the Republic of France prosperity and Consul General Méléaud and President Barre good health.

Dong and Cai Talk After Model Prison is Accused

The Caohejing Jiangsu Second Model Prison is very large and currently holds more than 2,000 prisoners, most of whom are political prisoners. Recently, the prison has been accused of being corrupt and inefficient, leading to dissatisfaction among the prisoners. Some days ago, prisoners Wang Jiaxiang, Lü Zongrui, and others specifically entrusted lawyer Dong Kang to present all the illegal and corrupt practices of the prison to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, requesting a thorough investigation and reform. Since lawyer Dong's petition was published in the newspapers, it has attracted great attention from all sectors of society. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency, considering that this matter concerns national legal system and human rights protection, specifically visited Mr. Dong Shoujing and Mr. Cai Ziming yesterday and received the following information:

Dong Shoujing Talks

The entrustment of this petition on behalf of Wang, Lü, and others is entirely due to the excessive and illegal ill-treatment they have suffered, and the appeal of Wang, Lü, and a few others can also be said to be the cry of all prisoners. Recently, there have been many rumors about prison corruption, so not long ago, I advised Wang Yuanzeng, Director of the Prison Affairs Department of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, in a personal capacity, to pay attention to the thorough investigation. It would be best to live with the prisoners for a week to fully understand the true situation in the prison. Mr. Wang agreed at the time. When I served as a prison official for two years during the Guangxu years 28 and 29, I was deeply aware of the darkness of our country's prisons. The extreme cruelty of the prison guards and jailers is truly indescribable. Therefore, when I later served in the judicial field, I made every effort to improve the situation. I visited prisons in Japan, Europe, and the United States, and everything was like heaven and earth compared to our country. In short, this problem is related to the entire national politics. If the politics are bad, the society will deteriorate, and there will be many lawbreakers, and the law enforcers will be in the same proportion. These are not local problems. I once saw a prison official in Suzhou who was young and did not know what the law was, but his actions were luxurious, none could surpass him. Later, I learned that this person was originally a relative of Wei Mingjun, the then Minister of Judicial Administration. At this point, I realized that officials today regard prison positions as lucrative jobs. If this is the case, how can we seek prison reform? However, this is just one aspect of the matter. Although I was entrusted with this petition by the prisoners due to my professional relationship, whether the allegations are true needs to be thoroughly investigated by the authorities. In my opinion, the corruption may be even worse than described in the petition. The lawyers' association will organize a prison inspection team, which is a mission that they should have in their profession. I have also heard that some members of the press have launched a reporter visit group. I think there is no need for excessive publicity, which would prevent the authorities from taking action. The Caohejing Prison Director has sent a letter to various newspapers, saying that the request should be based on facts and public opinion. This is very good. We will wait quietly for the true investigation and deeply hope that the authorities will correct their mistakes if they have them, and be more vigilant if they do not.

Cai Jiemin Talks

I have only seen Dong's lawyer's petition on behalf of the prisoners in the newspaper. Whether the allegations are true still needs to be investigated before a conclusion can be drawn. The charter of the Civil Rights Protection League originally stipulated the task of investigating prisons throughout the country. It was implemented once in Beiping. The lawyers' association will hold an inspection of Caohejing Prison, and the Civil Rights Protection League may not participate. As for when the League itself will investigate, it has not yet been decided.

Yu Hongjun Talks About the Concession Factory Inspection Issue

The Municipal Council Will Reply in Writing Within Days

It Will Not Tend to Extremes and Can Be Resolved by Compromise

Regarding the issue of the right to inspect factories in the Public Concession, Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun previously visited Municipal Council Chairman Fessenden to discuss the matter. According to Secretary-General Yu, who spoke to a reporter from the Central News Agency, he explained the attitude of the Chinese government to Mr. Fessenden. The Chinese government will not give up its sovereignty over the inspection of factories. If the Municipal Council ignores everything and implements inspections, it will be opposed by public opinion, and the Municipal Council will not be able to proceed smoothly. However, the Chinese government still hopes that the Municipal Council can assist in the process, adhering to the principle of not hindering Chinese sovereignty. Mr. Fessenden expressed sympathy for his statement and promised to consider it within a few days and reply in writing. According to Mr. Yu's observation, the Municipal Council will not always tend to extremes on this matter and a compromise can be reached.
