Lin Wo Jiang, Secretary-General of the Chinese Aviation Association, was summoned to Beijing by telegram by Ge Jingen, Secretary-General of the National Aviation Construction Association, on Monday (the 8th), and took the night train to Beijing to assist in preparing for the establishment of the Aviation Construction Association. The preparations have now been completed. He left Beijing by night train the night before and arrived in Shanghai at 8 a.m. yesterday. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited him at the Aviation Association yesterday afternoon and inquired about the recent progress of the establishment of the Aviation Construction Association and the Aviation Association's purchase of aircraft. Mr. Lin replied as follows:

Tasks of the Construction Association

The National Aviation Construction Association is an agency for fundraising, custody, and design, directly under the Executive Yuan. The government hires forty central committee members and leading figures from all walks of life and aviation personnel as directors, and appoints Song Ziwen, Zhu Peide, Qian Xinzhi, Shi Liangcai, and Ge Jingen as managing directors. Mr. Ge also serves as Secretary-General and is responsible for preparations. I am also a director. I went to Beijing on Monday at the summons of Director Ge and returned only yesterday. I spent four days in Beijing, assisting Director Ge in preparing for the establishment and drafting articles of association and proposals, which have been completed. The inaugural meeting is scheduled to be held at the Overseas Chinese Reception Center in Nanjing on the morning of the 20th. The association's office will be located at the original site of the Nanjing Aviation Administration (the Aviation Administration has now moved to Hangzhou). I will take the other directors from Shanghai to Beijing on the 19th to attend the inaugural meeting.

Aircraft Purchase Awaiting Funds

The Aviation Association has initially ordered twelve fighter jets. Since my last trip to Beijing to contact Vice Minister Chen of the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs, the type and configuration of the aircraft have been determined and will be ordered soon. However, the required funds are still insufficient from what has been raised in the city. The Shanghai Solicitation Team is working hard under the leadership of Mayor Wu, and although the results have only reached half of the intended goal, we feel that most of the donors are from the middle and lower classes. Getting this million is not easy. With Shanghai, a city concentrated with wealthy families, but the rich donate less, no wonder the income is not much. The extension has now been extended for one month. During this month, the Solicitation Team will focus its efforts on soliciting donations from the rich. The national situation is becoming increasingly dangerous, and the rich are certainly not ignorant of patriotism. A slight reduction in waste is already considerable. It is expected that the results obtained this month will exceed two million.

Rajchman, Chief of the Health Section of the League of Nations, previously accompanied Chinese Committee Member Li Shizeng to Nanchang to meet with Chairman Chiang to discuss matters related to China's health construction. After completing his official duties and returning to Beijing, he traveled to Shanghai with Li Shizeng, Liu Ruiheng, and others the day before. Mr. Rajchman's mission in China has been completed, and he took a boat to return to Europe yesterday morning.

The Richeng vessel of the Yongyuan Shipping Company, which encountered a reef outside Quanzhou around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday, was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday afternoon at approximately 4:00 PM, according to the shipping company, the Richeng vessel had successfully navigated out of danger yesterday morning and arrived in Quanzhou. However, one hold had taken on water, and the cargo was damaged. Unloading is currently underway. 宋慶齡等昨向德領館抗議

Song Qingling and Others Protested at the German Consulate Yesterday

Regarding Germany's Oppression of Civil Rights and Destruction of Culture

The China League for Civil Rights Protection, with the aim of promoting civil rights, regardless of international boundaries, has recently noted that since the rise to power of the Hitler faction in Germany, with its one-party dictatorship, innocent people have been persecuted, scholars have been oppressed, and the cruelty has been extreme. Therefore, yesterday (the 13th) morning, the Executive Committee, consisting of Song Qingling, Cai Yuanpei, Yang Xingfo, Lu Xun, and others, personally went to the German Consulate in this city to lodge a protest. They were received by Vice-Consul Mr. Bei Lian, who promised to forward the protest to the German Minister to China. The original text of the protest is as follows:

This League, based on reports in newspapers from various countries, has learned that since the Fascist Party came to power, the number of arrested workers has reached 30,000 to 40,000, while thousands of intellectuals have been subjected to oppression. Prisoners are subjected to brutal torture or killed, and afterwards it is falsely claimed that they committed suicide or were shot while attempting to escape. Corpses are frequently found in forests and rivers. Workers' organizations have been disbanded, and their property confiscated. Writers and scholars, due to their Jewish ethnicity or leftist political views, have been repeatedly subjected to various forms of humiliation. Scientists such as Einstein and Hirschfeld have been forced to leave the country. Famous writers, such as Ludwig Reun, Leon Feuchtwanger, and Thomas Mann, have either been forced to leave the country or subjected to extreme humiliation. The homes of great artists, such as Max Liebermann, and musicians, such as Bruno Walter, have been ransacked, and their manuscripts burned. The dark deeds of the Middle Ages in persecuting scientists, and the burning of books two thousand years ago, have unexpectedly reappeared today. Freedom of publication and speech has been completely deprived. Even journals of discussion, art, and literature, such as Weltbuehne, have been banned. The most right-wing New York Times (March 15th, 20th, and 21st) also reported the following: "The Vienna newspapers daily carry stories of the brutal torture of Communist, Socialist, Progressive, and Jewish members of parliament, journalists, writers, and lawyers." (Sollmann) "Beaten unconscious, ribs broken, and then their feet burned with fire. After waking up, they are beaten again." The teeth of the famous columnist "Ossietzky" were "knocked out with a pistol." "Heinz Pohl's novel manuscript was torn up and he was ordered to swallow it... In prison camps, prisoners are forced to fight each other until they pass out. In some cases, fathers and sons are forced to fight each other... Corpses are often found in the forests near Berlin every morning. Last week, three corpses were found in one day..." The above facts have been repeatedly reported in various newspapers of different political persuasions in Europe and America and are by no means one-sided accounts. This League believes that such inhumane acts not only trample on human rights but also oppress innocent scholars and writers, which is tantamount to destroying German culture. In the interests of humanity and the progress of society and culture, we hereby lodge the most serious protest.

According to Hua Dong News Agency, the recent outbreak of conflict in Guizhou has attracted widespread attention. Jiang Zaizhen's troops, after being directed by me, Jialie, to be temporarily stationed and reorganized in Houping and Yanhe, repeatedly received orders from the Central Government to proceed elsewhere, but they defied orders and instead gathered their forces to launch a fierce attack on Songtao, advancing to Zunyi, which led to a conflict with Tie Jian's (Hou Zhidan's) troops. The peace in Guizhou has been hindered. Thinking of the national crisis, I am deeply pained. I express my respect and gratitude. (Signed) Wang Jialie, with his seal affixed.

國際電台積極籌備中英通報

International Radio Station Actively Preparing for Sino-British Communication

運到機件一千餘件

Over One Thousand Components Arrived

眞茹瀏行添建鐵塔

Iron Towers Added in Zhenru and Liuhang

The International Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications, in preparation for Sino-British communication, has specially ordered one set each of transmitting and receiving equipment from the Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company of the United Kingdom and is constructing radio stations in Zhenru. The latest preparations of the station are detailed below:

機件續到

Continued Arrival of Components

The two sets of transmitting and receiving equipment ordered by the radio station from Marconi Company of the United Kingdom, valued at 500,000 gold pounds, equivalent to over 800,000 Chinese dollars, have been delivered in three batches. Yesterday, the fourth batch arrived from the United Kingdom. According to the station, the four batches of large and small machines that have arrived so far total 1,500 pieces, most of which are for external applications. The remaining internal application components are currently being shipped and are expected to be fully delivered by the end of July.

添建鐵塔

Addition of Iron Towers

The international radio stations in Zhenru and Liuhang already have several antenna towers. In order to expand its communication capabilities, the station is adding three antenna towers in Zhenru and five in Liuhang. Each tower is 160 feet tall and construction has already begun. It is expected to be completed by October.

年底通報

Communication by Year's End

The station considers that its existing buildings are insufficient for Sino-British communication, so it is adding several buildings in Zhenru to house the Sino-British communication equipment. Since construction began, the external works have been largely completed. The equipment shipped from the UK is expected to be installed starting at the end of July and completed by mid-September. The clarity of the signal will need to be tested for one or two months, so the communication period is expected to be no earlier than the end of the year.

The Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs and the Commissioner of Customs issued an announcement yesterday stating: "For the purpose of announcement, in accordance with the government's instructions, all imported goods that were previously exempt from customs surcharges and disaster relief surcharges (see this customs' announcement of November 27th, 1931),

from the 16th of this month, the aforementioned two surcharges will be levied in all cases. Goods stored in customs warehouses will also be subject to these taxes without exception, and no extensions will be granted. All merchants are hereby informed. This announcement is hereby made."

鄧眞德注意兩路防疫事宜

Deng Zhende Pays Attention to Epidemic Prevention on Both Railways

爲鐵路人員及乘客免費注射

Free Injections for Railway Staff and Passengers

隨時與衛生機關大規模防範

Large-Scale Prevention with Health Authorities at Any Time

Deng Zhende, Medical Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, in order to prevent the spread of epidemics during the summer and autumn seasons of this year, led his staff and cleaning inspectors from the two railway administrations to inspect the medical and health conditions of various stations and factories along the two lines. Since the two railways are important transportation hubs, epidemics can spread rapidly if they occur near the railway lines. Therefore, prevention efforts have been advanced this year to provide free vaccinations to railway employees, their families, and passengers, and seven epidemic prevention measures have been formulated for effective implementation: (1) Free vaccinations for employees, their families, and passengers; (2) Compilation and distribution of picture brochures, slogans, and pamphlets on epidemic prevention for display in stations and trains and distribution to passengers to promote awareness; (3) Production and distribution of emergency antiseptic lotions; (4) Requesting assistance from railway and police personnel in cleaning inspections and from doctors in clinics in handling epidemic prevention matters, as well as banning vendors from selling unsanitary food and beverages on trains and at stations; (5) Dispatching epidemic prevention personnel to inspect and administer vaccines on trains when necessary; (6) Cooperating and coordinating with other local medical and health authorities for prevention; (7) In the event of an epidemic outbreak, consulting with the Ministry of Interior's Health Department and the Municipal Health Bureau at any time for large-scale prevention efforts. It is reported that since serving on the two railways, Mr. Deng has devoted himself to designing and improving the medical and health services of the two railways, and his achievements have been remarkable.

賑委會再撥萬元振濟蘇馬等部眷屬

Prohibiting Shops from Using Musical Instruments

感無線電號召主顧

And Radio to Attract Customers

The French Municipal Council, in order to address the practice of shops in the French Concession using musical instruments or radio to attract customers, has newly established regulations for the management of musical instrument advertisements, which are now in effect. The regulations are transcribed below. Shanghai French Concession Municipal Council Regulations for the Management of Musical Instrument Advertisements. Article 1: All shops or other publicly accessible institutions that use sound-producing musical instruments, such as phonographs, radio broadcasting machines, and other musical instruments, with the aim of attracting crowds, thereby obstructing traffic or disturbing nearby residents, must immediately cease playing upon notification by the police. Article 2: Those who violate these regulations will be subject to a fine of one to ten yuan.

明日起市輪渡展遲末班時間

City Ferry Extends and Delays Last Ferry Departure Time Starting Tomorrow

市輪渡每逢夏季、乘客特别擁擠、均以滬上人士赴浦東鄕郊游覽者居多、所備渡輪、不敷應用、内赴浦東高橋者、均由滬陸續前往、旁晚整批返滬、倘阻其登輪、則一部分乘客、勢將無法返滬、應付殊感困難、公用局有鑒於此、曾經計劃更大更快渡輪一艘、以資補救、但因種種關係、開工較遲、本年夏季、不能完成、故另行設法、自本星期日（五月十四日）起、將上午五時三十分、由高橋開上海之一班、及原有末班下午六時三十分、改爲下午七時十分、由高橋開上海之一班、均用兩輪、同時行駛、以免擁塞、此項辦法、業由公用局輪渡總管理處、用中西文發出通告云、

The city ferry is particularly crowded every summer, mostly due to people from Shanghai visiting the countryside of Pudong. The available ferries are insufficient to meet the demand. Those going to Gaoqiao in Pudong travel continuously from Shanghai and return in batches in the evening. If they are prevented from boarding, some passengers will be unable to return to Shanghai, making it difficult to cope. In view of this, the Public Utilities Bureau had planned a larger and faster ferry to remedy the situation, but due to various reasons, the start of construction was delayed and it will not be completed this summer. Therefore, other measures have been taken. Starting from this Sunday (May 14), the 5:30 AM ferry from Gaoqiao to Shanghai and the original last ferry at 6:30 PM will be changed to 7:10 PM, and the ferry from Gaoqiao to Shanghai will use two ferries running simultaneously to avoid congestion. The Public Utilities Bureau's Ferry Management Office has issued a notice in Chinese and Western languages about this measure.

French Concession Inspects Prostitutes Within the Concession

法租界當局近爲，於界内各妓院避免傅染梅毒起見、傅諭各妓女、一律由醫生檢騐各已略誌前報、茲　昨日由法捕房發出通告、及關於妓院内僱妓衛生章程、派探分送各妓院、照錄如下、通告、（一）妓院内之寄娼妓、以後必須按時騐病、目的爲避免梅、或别種傅染病之蔓延、（二）法工部局委派醫生按時檢騐、并由捕房檢查、（三）給每妓特種册子上貼妓女照相登錄末次騐病結果、及其日期、此册客人皆可索閱、如彼能確定妓院内之妓女衛生現狀、（四）不准妓院主人、僱用院外婦女、無照或其執照已被捕房撤去之妓女、（五）客人應拒絕一切婦女不能出示其必備之捕房執照、且能報告捕房、凡該妓反對呈出執照、（關於妓院内僱妓衛生章程）（一）禁止妓院主人、僱用或容留身患傅染疾病之妓女（二）警務處總監、得隨時命醫生騐視院内妓女、（三）凡妓女一經騐出患有傅染病者、捕房得立刻吊銷其執照、并得處罰院主、每一病妓、五元至五十元之罰金、如有累犯不悛者、捕房得將妓院封閉、妓院内婦女、必須騐病、實　預防梅毒之蔓延、故院主尤應注意其院内居留各妓、對於身體上應具充分之衛生、若使狎客在彼處染疾、則有損該院之名譽、妓女患恙時、尤應立告其主人、因除規定騐病日　外、彼等遇有疑難、亦可請示醫生防範、衛生其法至簡、常以消毒、或止爛藥品洗滌、即能阻禦多種病症之傅染、惟院主務須催促其妓女殷勤清洗、並不得使形似染疾、或不潔之妓女遲疑騐病云、

The French Concession authorities have recently ordered that all prostitutes in brothels within the concession be examined by doctors in order to prevent the spread of syphilis, as previously reported. The French police issued a notice yesterday, along with sanitary regulations for prostitutes working in brothels, and sent detectives to distribute them to all brothels. The contents are transcribed below: Notice: (1) Prostitutes working in brothels must undergo regular medical examinations in the future to prevent the spread of syphilis or other infectious diseases. (2) The French Municipal Council will appoint doctors to conduct regular examinations, which will also be inspected by the police. (3) Each prostitute will be given a special booklet with her photo and the results and date of her last examination. Customers can request to see this booklet so they can determine the current health status of the prostitutes in the brothel. (4) Brothel owners are not allowed to hire women from outside the brothel, or prostitutes without a license or whose licenses have been revoked by the police. (5) Customers should refuse any woman who cannot produce her required police license and should report to the police if the prostitute refuses to present her license. (Sanitary Regulations for Prostitutes Working in Brothels) (1) Brothel owners are prohibited from hiring or harboring prostitutes suffering from infectious diseases. (2) The Commissioner of Police may order a doctor to examine the prostitutes in the brothel at any time. (3) If a prostitute is found to have an infectious disease, the police may immediately revoke her license and fine the brothel owner five to fifty yuan for each infected prostitute. If there are repeated offenses, the police may close the brothel. It is essential for women in brothels to undergo medical examinations to prevent the spread of syphilis. Therefore, brothel owners should pay particular attention to the hygiene of their residents and ensure that their bodies are thoroughly clean. If customers contract an illness there, it will damage the brothel's reputation. Prostitutes should immediately inform their owners when they are ill. In addition to the scheduled examination days, they can also consult doctors for advice on prevention if they encounter any difficulties. The method of hygiene is very simple and can often be achieved by disinfecting or washing with wound-healing medicines, which can prevent the transmission of many diseases. However, brothel owners must urge their prostitutes to wash diligently and must not allow prostitutes who appear to be infected or unclean to delay medical examinations.

先致壽儀二金繼卽開槍殺人

Presented Birthday Gifts of Two Dollars First, Then Opened Fire and Killed

顧道生爲岳父做壽送命

Gu Daosheng Gave His Life for His Father-in-Law's Birthday Celebration

兇手孫殿臣在旅館被逮

The Murderer Sun Dianchen Was Arrested in a Hotel

Gu Daosheng, also known as Yuesheng, age 27, from Nanxiang, the son-in-law of Jin Liuting, a blind man from Jiaxing who lives at No. 277 Wangjia Wharf in Nanshi and works as a fortune teller, used to be a boatman, but now works as a dock insurance cargo watcher. On March 26th of this year, for the 60th birthday of his father-in-law, Jin Liuting, Gu booked the Dajilou restaurant at No. 57 Xiaodongmen Street in the French Concession to hold a birthday banquet. That afternoon, suddenly, an intruder, pretending to be delivering gifts, entered the door at 4:20 PM and exchanged a few words of pleasantries with Gu, then handed him two dollars as a gift, turned around and went outside. Gu escorted him to the second doorway, and the guest turned around, pulled out a pistol, and fired at Gu, fatally wounding him. The murderer escaped on the spot. Later, the police took the body in a hearse for an autopsy. After the court confirmed the cause of death, the widow, Gu Jinshi, signed for the body to be collected and buried, while the police investigated and apprehended the murderer. Now, Jin Jiulin, a detective supervisor from the French police, and Zhang Ziying, a police detective, have found that the murderer of Gu is Sun Dianchen, from Jiangbei, who is hiding in a room in the Laodongfang Hotel at the intersection of Sanma Road and Zhejiang Road in the Public Concession. They, together with Chinese and Western detectives from the Laozha Police Station, rushed to the hotel at 4:30 AM yesterday and arrested Sun. They took him back to the police station and escorted him to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court at noon. At 3:00 PM, Judge Xiong Huiping conducted a preliminary hearing. Gu Shouxi, the police lawyer, stated that the police had found that the defendant was related to the murder of Gu Daosheng, so he was arrested. Due to the lack of time, the investigation had not yet been completed, and he requested a postponement of two weeks to allow for a thorough investigation. The court asked the defendant about his age, origin, occupation, and address, and then granted the postponement for another hearing. The defendant was remanded in custody.

The Murderer of the Young Master of Qian Fengtai Firm Arrested Yesterday Morning

丨 Lu Quanxing from Wuxi 丨

Chen Zhikui, a native of Ningbo and the young master of Qian Fengtai Incense and Candle Shop located at No. 52 Xinqiao Street in the French Concession, was 29 years old this year. On the afternoon of the 14th of last month, he delivered goods to Hongkou to be shipped to Hankou via river steamer. After finishing his business, he returned to the shop at 9:00 PM. Shortly after, he turned to go out, taking a detour through a small alley next to the north side of the building. As he entered his home through the back door upstairs, he was unexpectedly confronted by a thug in the alley who opened fire with a pistol. He was struck in the throat by a bullet and died instantly. The store's accountant, surnamed Chen, was also wounded. The assailant fled into Baoyu Lane on the spot. The injured person was then taken to the hospital for treatment by the patrolmen, and the body was transported to the coroner's office. After the court sent officials to conduct an examination, the family claimed the body for burial, awaiting the patrolmen to apprehend the murderer and bring him to justice. All of these details were previously reported in the newspaper. It is now learned that Jin Jiulin, an inspector of the special agency of the French patrol, has discovered that the murderer of Chen was Lu Quanxing, a 20-year-old man from Wuxi, who was hiding at No. 40, Shuang Gui Li, Rue du Père Froc. Therefore, at 8:00 AM yesterday morning, he led detectives and quietly went to arrest Lu. A pistol and several bullets used in the crime were found. He was taken to the patrol station, interrogated by the detective chief, and then escorted to the Second Special District Local Court at noon for investigation. At 2:30 PM, Judge Tai Huiping, accompanied by court clerk Tao Zongkan, presided over the hearing in the First Criminal Court. First, Gu Shouxi, the patrol's lawyer, stated the case, saying that the patrol had arrested the defendant for murder, but due to time constraints, a detailed investigation of the case had not been possible. He requested that the defendant be detained temporarily and that the case be investigated and prosecuted after two weeks. The court verified the statement, questioned Lu, and then approved the postponement of the trial for further investigation. The defendant was returned to custody.

Fatal Surgery for Scrofula

丨 Cheng Zhankui Dies Tragically at the Hands of an Incompetent Doctor 丨

Cheng Zhankui, a 42-year-old man from Shandong, worked as a driver for the French-owned Tram Company. However, he was fond of women, which recently led to him contracting scrofula and syphilis. He kept this a secret, fearing that it would become known and he would be disgraced. He stayed alone at the Aido Hotel on West Xinqiao Road, and hired Liu Baokun from Tianjin, who ran the Yongqing Tang medical clinic on Baliqiao Street in the French Concession, for treatment. At around 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, Liu performed surgery on Cheng in the clinic, making an incision to treat the scrofula. Unexpectedly, Liu used the knife too forcefully and severed an artery in Cheng's leg, causing Cheng to bleed profusely and turn pale. Liu, realizing his mistake, quickly sent Cheng back to the Aido Hotel. However, the hotel's tea server noticed that Cheng was in critical condition and immediately reported it to the Great World clock tower police station. Detectives took Cheng to Renji Hospital, but he died en route due to excessive blood loss. The body was taken to the coroner's office for examination, and a detective was dispatched to arrest the incompetent doctor Liu Baokun for investigation.

500 Japanese Marines Return Home

Those Who Participated in the Shanghai Invasion War

Five hundred replacement soldiers of the Japanese Marines stationed in Shanghai departed from the Marine Headquarters on Jiangwan Road at 9:00 AM yesterday morning. They traveled via North Sichuan Road, Peng Road, and Huade Road to the Osaka Wharf, boarded a special service ship, and set sail for Sasebo at around 11:00 AM. These replacement soldiers had all participated in the invasion of Shanghai, so many Japanese expatriates went to the wharf to see them off. When they passed North Sichuan Road, Japanese elementary school students stood on the east side of the road, from Aruicheng all the way to Yokohama Bridge, waving flags and cheering, which greatly offended the Chinese.

Li Zhengwu's Coffin Scheduled to Be Transported to Ningbo

Departure from Shanghai on the 16th

After Mr. Li Zhengwu, a prominent figure in Shanghai, passed away in his Shanghai residence last month, the Ningbo Fellow-Countrymen Association in Shanghai organized a funeral committee to handle all matters. It is now learned that Mr. Li's coffin will depart from Shanghai on the 16th and arrive in Ningbo on the 17th. Ningbo gentry and scholars, recognizing his contributions to the party and the country and his great achievements, have established three public memorial sites: (1) at the Jiangtian Wharf in Ningbo, (2) on Jiangnan Street in Zhenhai, and (3) in Pumiandi. The French Concession Residents' Association Asks the Municipal Council to Waive the Awning Tax

Since the French Concession announced the collection of an awning tax, the general merchants and residents believe that the purpose of awnings is to shield from the sun, which is beneficial and harmless to pedestrians. Furthermore, the time they are used is short, and it is not appropriate to levy taxes on them, which would increase the burden on merchants and residents. Therefore, the French Concession Residents' Association sent a letter to the French Municipal Council yesterday, requesting them to revoke their decision. The original text is as follows: Firstly, according to a letter from the Second District Branch, the French Municipal Council has notified all businesses that they must pay awning tax from May of this year. The awnings used by stores are to shield from the sunlight for the benefit of pedestrians. Moreover, the awnings are only used for a few hours each day. In cloudy, rainy weather and during the spring and winter, they are not used at all. Now, the French Municipal Council is using the word "awning" as a reason to collect a large amount of tax, which businesses can hardly afford. We request that your council quickly advocate with the French Municipal Council to rescind this awning tax. The use of awnings is originally for shielding from the sunlight and does not obstruct pedestrians. Taxing them is inappropriate. According to the aforementioned situation, we request that your council consider the difficulties of businesses and revoke the decision to reassure businesses and alleviate the difficulties of merchants. Respectfully submitted.

The Famous Female Doctor Huang Qiongxian Will Be Buried Today

Dr. Huang Qiongxian was the sister of Huang Tingzuo, the former supervisor of students studying in the United States, and the sister of the late wife of President Bu of St. John's University. Huang studied at St. Mary's School in her youth, and then studied medicine at Tongren Hospital in Hongkou. Later, she went to Canada for further studies, graduated, and returned to China. She was highly regarded by the authorities and hired as a doctor in the hospital founded by Duanfang. After the revolution, she practiced medicine in Shanghai. With her deep knowledge and countless lives saved, she enjoyed a great reputation. However, she had diabetes and recently developed a tumor on her waist. After repeated treatments, she passed away on the 7th of this month due to her advanced age and weakened body. It is now learned that her family has chosen 3:00 PM today to hold a funeral service at the St. John's University Chapel in Fanwangdu. After the funeral, the hearse will depart, pass through Jessfield Road and enter Great Western Road, cross Columbia Road, and go to the International Cemetery on Hongqiao Road for burial.

Jiangxi Porcelain Publicly Displayed for the Chicago Expo

China has been preparing for the Chicago Expo for a year, and the products from various provinces have been very enthusiastic. However, due to the government's concerns about the pressing national crisis, the decision was made to stop participating. The producers from various provinces requested the government's guidance and subsidies to participate on their own. More than 400 boxes of exhibits have been shipped out in two batches, as reported in this newspaper. Jiangxi porcelain has the largest quantity of exhibits from various provinces. In addition to the 200 boxes that have already been shipped, there are still dozens of pieces left. Due to packaging and re-boxing procedures, they could not be completed in time, and it is planned to ship them in the third batch. They include a porcelain statue of Premier Sun Yat-sen, 12 feet tall, and dozens of magnetic models made in Jingdezhen. The magnetic models depict the porcelain-making process from the kiln to the coloring, with lifelike figures, which are unique to all past exhibits. In addition, there are also hundreds of other famous and precious porcelain pieces, such as blue-and-white and copper-red vases, and longevity plates made during Empress Dowager Cixi's birthday. Before being shipped, the representatives of the province contacted the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and temporarily displayed them on the third floor of the chamber's commodity exhibition hall for the public to view. Recently, the weather has been clear and sunny, and the number of tourists in the city has also increased significantly.

Opening News of the China Cultural Relics Museum

The owner of Daoyi Studio, who is knowledgeable and fond of antiquities, has collected famous paintings, calligraphy, bronze ware, jade, cultural relics, and carvings for more than ten years, numbering in the thousands. In order to spread the culture and art of China from ancient times, he has printed the Cultural Relics Monthly magazine. All the items published in it are rare and valuable works of art from the private sector, which are not commonly seen in the market. The owner has traveled north and south for several months to bring it to fruition. He also hopes to make more friends and has established the China Cultural Relics Museum at No. 10 Wangjiasha, Huayuan Road in this city, divided into publishing and distribution departments. In addition to the first issue of Cultural Relics, which has already been published, he is also continuously compiling and printing other famous and valuable ink rubbings, collections of paintings and inscriptions, and couplets in four calligraphic styles. The distribution department has opened a room to display the owner's own collections and also collects secret items from old friends and collectors, marking the value and making it public to connoisseurs. In the past ten days, archaeological appraisers such as Ye Yuhu, Xu Shuyi, Fei Jingzhong, and Sun Zhongkuan, and painters such as Huang Ainong, Yi Dachang, Qin Qingzeng, He Tianjian, Qian Shoutie, and Wang Fu'an have all visited, praised, and purchased items.

Wang Thirtyzi Transferred to Shanghai Local Court

The Wanted Criminal in the Assassination of Ji Zhongtang

Wang Thirtyzi, a native of Yancheng, Jiangbei, used to be a vagrant on Hujiamu Bridge in Hongkou. During the January 28th Incident, that area became an enemy-occupied zone. As a result, he opened a gambling den and indulged in debauchery, taking advantage of the situation to rise up. Ji Zhongtang, who had been a detective and had just been released from prison, wanted to get a share of the pie, which led to a conflict. Wang and his accomplices shot and killed Ji. At that time, it was in the Japanese-controlled area, so there was no way to investigate. After the ceasefire agreement was concluded, those who had relied on the enemy's power lost their protection. Therefore, Wang was wanted by the local court. Wang fled to the concession and did not hide his tracks. A detective found a pistol on him, and the patrolmen escorted him to the First Special District Local Court. After investigation, it was found that he had committed previous crimes, so he was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment. The local court then learned of this and sent a document to the First Court through Chief Prosecutor Lou, ordering the police to bring him to court. After a preliminary hearing by the original prosecutor Yang An, he ordered him to be detained pending a confrontation with the victim's family.

Woman Swallows Opium and Is Rescued; Investigation into the Source of the Opium Leads to a Sentence

At around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, Li Shi, a woman from Jiangbei living in a flat in Xinji Bang Road, swallowed opium after quarreling with her husband over a minor matter. She secretly went to Yanzike at No. 257 Huaji Road, bought two jiao of opium, and took it home to commit suicide. Someone noticed and sent her to Tongren Hospital. Because she had only been poisoned for a short time, she was saved by the doctor. She was then discharged from the hospital. The Huishan patrol station learned of this and sent Chinese detective Fu Bingzang to investigate. He learned the source of the opium and arrested Liang Kairi, a native of Ningbo who sold the opium on Huaji Road. He was taken to the patrol station along with the opium pipe and opium paste. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Local Court. Judge Xiao Xiefen presided over the hearing. The patrol lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated, "The fact of this case is that Li Shi, a woman from Jiangbei, swallowed opium and committed suicide after a minor quarrel with her paramour. Fortunately, she was saved by the doctor, otherwise her life would have been in danger. She should be severely punished." Detective Fu then reported the circumstances of the case and presented the opium pipe and other items for inspection. When questioned, the defendant denied having a private opium den. The patrol lawyer claimed that the defendant was identified by Li Shi at the patrol station yesterday as the person from whom she bought the opium she swallowed. There was no room for denial. After Judge Xiao verified the confession, he sentenced Liang Kairi to one year in prison as a warning. The confiscated opium paraphernalia was confiscated.

Female Corpse Found on Wanzhu Road

Yesterday morning at dawn, a patrolman discovered a female corpse on Huaizhen Street, Wanzhu Road, Nine Acres. It was determined that she was about 40 years old, had her hair tied up, and wore mourning clothes. She was wearing a black calico short shirt and pants and had a gold tooth in her mouth. Her waist was tied with a hemp rope, there was a bloody knife wound behind her right ear, and there were injuries on her body. It was believed that she had been murdered and the body moved to the location. The case was reported to the First Precinct of the Second District, which ordered Jiang Pingyang of Jiupu to report to the local court for an examination. Prosecutor Yang and others arrived at the scene and confirmed that it was a murder. He ordered that the body be collected and that the murderer be apprehended and brought to justice after the family members identified the body.

After the Dahua Wool Company Closed Down, Shareholders Accuse the Manager of Breach of Trust and Embezzlement

丨 Listing Eight Items of Malpractice 丨

Dr. Shen Zhongfang, also known as Shen Baoyi, partnered with Zhu Xiaofeng and others last autumn to open the Dahua Wool Company on Guangdong Road, with a total capital of 30,000 yuan, divided into three shares. Shen and Zhu each took one share, and the remaining share was taken by a Mr. Sun. Zhu was appointed as the manager. The company opened on July 26th and closed down in November, operating for only four months and incurring heavy losses. Recently, Shen hired a lawyer to file a criminal complaint against Zhu for embezzlement and breach of trust, listing eight items of malpractice: (1) Embezzling 735 taels and 5 qian of silver received from Hengtongzhuang, and falsely claiming it was paid into the account of Shen Zhongji; (2) Setting up temporary entries to embezzle more than 1,240 yuan; (3) Arbitrarily defaulting on payments, reaching more than 4,400 yuan by the time of closure; (4) More than 5,000 yuan paid for fixed assets was mostly unreal; (5) The maximum amount of defaulted payments was 4,670 taels of silver and 8,400 yuan in foreign currency; (6) His account owed Dahua more than 300 yuan, while he counterclaimed 1,460 taels of silver; (7) Extravagantly spending 1,000 yuan on travel expenses and 200 yuan on entertainment expenses; (8) Purchasing cotton from Tianjin at a high price and selling it at a low price, resulting in a loss of more than 6,000 yuan. The First Special District Local Court had already held a hearing, but because both the plaintiff and the defendant intended to settle the matter, the hearing was postponed. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Tingqi continued the hearing, ordering both parties to appear in court and inquiring about the settlement situation. According to the plaintiff Shen Baoyi, the defendant was not sincere about the settlement, so it could not be resolved outside the court. The court then ordered the plaintiff to state the facts of the eight items of malpractice one by one, and then questioned the defendant Zhu Xiaofeng, who defended against each item. Judge Wu verified the confession and stated that the case was purely a dispute over accounts and should first be filed with the civil court for review. He then ordered that the case be suspended and that the plaintiff file a lawsuit with the civil court for review.

Robbery of a Cigarette and Paper Shop on North Shanxi Road; Perpetrator Arrested

丨 Many Arms and Ammunition Confiscated 丨

The Ruixiang cigarette and paper shop at No. 494 North Shanxi Road was suddenly broken into by several armed bandits at 9:45 PM on the 28th of last month, who robbed large and small silver dollars. The owner reported the incident to the patrol station and requested that they be investigated. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, Chinese detective Shen Afu of the Huisi patrol station arrested Gu Zhanglong and Wang Rongzhang (also known as Jiajia), two bandits involved in the case, at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Bazilu Road. A pistol and 29 bullets were found at No. 2, Gujiazhai, Zhabei. They were taken to the patrol station and detained. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First District Court. Patrol lawyer Li Zhishan stated the case, saying that the case still needed to be investigated and requested permission to detain them. The two defendants admitted that they and a certain Jia, who was still at large, went to rob, with Wang acting as a lookout and Gu taking action inside. Judge Qian Wenji verified the confession and ordered that Gu and Wang be detained pending a further hearing in seven days.

Prevention of Cholera and Leprosy

The Chief of the Health Department of the Public Works Bureau reported to the Health Committee that he had attended the cholera prevention conference convened in Shanghai on the 8th of this month. The conference also discussed the issue of clean water supply. Last year, the water company provided free water, and it is hoped that the company can cooperate this year as well. The residents of shantytowns benefited greatly from this clean water last year, but its effectiveness cannot be demonstrated by statistical methods.

Regarding the prevention of leprosy, the Chief of the Health Department also reported that an association has been established for this purpose in China, and it is planned to establish one or two clinics in Shanghai in the future, as well as a sanatorium in the countryside. Patients should be prevented from moving from other cities to Shanghai. A conference will be held in Nanjing this autumn to discuss prevention issues. The starting point should be the collection of statistics. Currently, the nearest leprosy sanatorium is only in Hangzhou, and it is very difficult to move Shanghai patients there.

Inspection Report of the China Reclamation Bank

The China Reclamation Bank issued an inspection report on its reserves, stating that the issuance reserve and the business reserve of the China Reclamation Bank have always been completely separated. According to the bank's articles of association, the cash reserve should be above 70% and the guarantee reserve should be below 30%. On the 13th of this month, accountant Wang Zikang, together with directors Xu Jiqing and Xu Busun, representatives of the board of supervisors, conducted an inspection. The results are as follows: total amount of exchange coupons issued: 4,779,000 silver dollars; total amount of exchange coupon reserve: 4,779,000 silver dollars, including: cash reserve: 3,751,288 silver dollars; guarantee reserve: 1,027,712 silver dollars. The above two items show that the cash reserve accounts for slightly more than 78%, and the guarantee reserve accounts for slightly less than 22%. This report is specifically made.

City News

▲ Advantages of Huasheng Fan from National Goods Factory Hua Sheng Electric Appliance Manufacturing Factory started manufacturing electric fans in the 8th year of the Republic of China, after 14 years of experience, each year's products have considerable reforms in manufacturing. The speed of progress and the precision of the structure are unparalleled, and the most important internal structure of the fan is the shaft collar (i.e. front and rear bosses) at both ends of the motor. The factory initially used extremely fine special copper material, placed in between. However, after a long period of use, the volume of the fan generated heat, so it was changed to steel ball shaft collar. After a long time of testing, the result was that the heat was not reduced, but a rustling sound was generated, which was very loud. Whether in the office or at home, it was very uncomfortable to hear. Mr. Yang Jichuan, the chief engineer of the factory, after several studies, used a chemical method to combine a metal compound of copper to make the shaft collar. Therefore, the fans that are now on the market have metal compound copper installed in the front and rear bosses, which do not generate heat and have no noise. This is the advantage of the Huasheng fan from the National Goods Factory.

To Whom It May Concern, In the news about the reconstruction of the Shanghai North Railway Station published in your newspaper on the 8th of this month, it was stated that the project was contracted by the Jiangnan Construction Company. This was also published in your newspaper's construction special issue on the 9th. After investigation, the project was actually contracted by our company. The content published in your newspaper is not accurate, which has caused misunderstandings in the outside world. Please correct it immediately. Sincerely, Shanghai Zhongnan Construction Company, 22.5.13.

To the esteemed Editor, With all due respect, I recently read in your newspaper a news item about President Wang denying sending a representative to Guangdong, which involved my name and greatly affects my personal reputation. In addition to writing directly to President Wang, I have enclosed the original letter to President Wang and would like to ask you to publish it to clarify the truth. I am grateful. Sincerely, Wang Xiaoya, May 13.

Attached is Wang Xiaoya's original letter to President Wang, Dear Mr. Jingwei, I recently read in the newspaper that in your telegram to Commander-in-Chief Chen Jitang, you mentioned someone named "Wang Xiaoya" impersonating your representative. My name is "Xiaoya", and the characters "Ya" and "Ya" are different. Perhaps there is another Wang Xiaoya, but my relatives and friends often mistakenly write "Ya" as "Ya", so I must solemnly declare to avoid misunderstandings. After investigation, the Shanghai Shenbao reported on the 8th of this month that a telegram from Hong Kong said that Wang's representative Xiaoya went to Guangdong to discuss the Lin Quan Conference, while the Xinwen Bao's exclusive telegram said that Wang's representative Xiao Chong went to Guangdong. Your speech in Nanjing on the 10th denying the dispatch of representatives also referred to "Xiao Chong". I thought that the Hong Kong telegram "Xiaoya" published in Shenbao might be a mistake for "Xiao Chong", so I did not correct it. However, your telegram suddenly changed Xiao Chong to Wang Xiaoya. Is it because of rumor mongering and you did not investigate thoroughly? Or is there someone else? I don't know. As for me, I have my own revolutionary position and would not impersonate the representative of an important person. In addition to publishing a solemn statement in Shen Xin and other newspapers, I should ask you to find out the truth and quell the rumors, and also ask you to order the Central News Agency to send a letter to correct it, which would be greatly appreciated.

National Shame Week Lecture by Mr. Shen Tilan on the May 3rd Massacre

Lecture at the YMCA on May 10th

The chairman just said that I went to Jinan to investigate the May 3rd Massacre after it happened. I did go there once, but this will disappoint you, I only saw the surface. For example, Japanese soldiers running rampant on the streets, recklessly. I couldn't see the reasons, situation, and international relations that constituted this massacre in Jinan. I also have very little research on history. Today, I just spent an hour after school to briefly think about the before and after of this massacre, and talk to you about it.

In the autumn of the 15th year of the Republic of China, the National Revolutionary Army swore an oath to launch the Northern Expedition from Guangzhou. Within a few months, it reached Wuhan, Jiangxi, and Nanjing in March of the 16th year: The rapid military progress during this period was amazing. However, the National Revolution only reached Nanjing. Due to the xenophobic actions of some troops, imperialism incited a demonstration on the pretext, which caused the Nanjing Incident. Later, the Ninghan split, and the Nanjing government held a crackdown on the Communist Party, which caused a setback for the National Revolution in its very smooth journey in the Northern Expedition. In April of the same year, the National Revolutionary Army continued to advance northward from Nanjing along the Jinpu Railway. The Japanese who held power at the time were the Tanaka Cabinet, a cabinet manipulated by a militaristic warlord. He believed that the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army was a sweeping away of Japan's rights and interests in North China, so he resolutely sent troops from Qingdao to land. In order to avoid conflict, the Nanjing government kept its troops in Xuzhou and stopped going north. Seeing that there was no opportunity to take advantage of, the Japanese warlords had to withdraw their troops back in September. When the National Revolutionary Army continued the Northern Expedition in April of the 17th year, Japan again sent troops to Qingdao and attacked Jinan to the west. After the National Revolutionary Army came into contact with the Japanese army, Jinan was lost in less than two days. Two months later, what I saw in Jinan was only Japanese cavalry galloping everywhere, Japanese soldiers arbitrarily breaking into houses or shops to search, and prohibiting Chinese people from walking together in groups of three or five. What I saw in Jinan was a piece of land that had become a conquered country for a period of time, and the people of Jinan had become slaves for a period of time.

Ten months later, the National Revolutionary Army went north again and occupied Tianjin and Beiping. Zhang Zuolin, who was outside the customs, wanted to maintain his power in the north, so he entered the customs to resist, but later he was bombed to death by the Japanese in HuangguTun. This kind of action of bombing to death a Chinese warlord also shows Japan's dissatisfaction with the old-style Chinese warlords, and he wanted to find an opportunity to find another suitable puppet tool.

At this time, a local unification was achieved. By the end of the year, Zhang Xueliang and the inside of the pass exchanged news, informally accepting the efforts of the National Revolution to develop outside the pass: In June of the following year, the Liaoning Provincial Government was formally established, accepting the Three Principles of the People and hanging the Qing Tian Bai Ri flag. At this point, China was unified.

The Japanese troops in Jinan were withdrawn after negotiations, also in April of the second year. It is said that the withdrawal of troops was conditional. The general public naturally does not care how Japan would withdraw its troops.

These are the before and after circumstances of the May 3rd Massacre.

We believe that commemorating a painful national humiliation does not lie in the recollection of the facts themselves, but in focusing on investigating the causes, significance, and relations in which the massacre occurred. We believe that this can increase the significance of the commemoration, and only in this way can we recognize the road ahead and understand our responsibilities.

Now I will talk about it in four parts:

1. The May 3rd Massacre and Japan's Internal Affairs

Japan is a newly emerging imperialist country, and the feudal consciousness of their domestic warlords is very strong. Their power often exceeds that of the government, and they are certainly advocating aggression against China. On the other hand, Japan is also a newly emerging capitalist country, and the power of the domestic capitalist class (financial groups) is equal to that of the warlords, and they are also advocating aggression against China. However, although these two factions have the same purpose of aggression against China, their methods are different. The warlords advocate using force to invade, flaunting the prestige of their militaristic militarism, while the financial groups advocate using economic means to invade, so that China is unknowingly subjected to their oppression. The financial groups advocate this way, seeing the superficial compromise of the powers at the time for the Chinese revolution, believing that only by prospering China can they invade China. This contradictory law is correct and can be said in their own country. However, the warlords believe that economic aggression is not painful enough. On the one hand, they use the large number of unemployed people in the country and the demands of the petty bourgeoisie to call for the development of the Far East and the expansion of colonies, and carry out their militaristic militarism dreams. The cannon of May 3rd is the beginning of exposing the internal conflicts of Japanese imperialism! And the rise of warlord power?

A year later, when the Japanese troops withdrew from Jinan, the majority of the Japanese people and the bourgeoisie saw that the effect of military aggression was not so good, and many criticized the warlords. The Japanese warlords originally wanted to use the Chinese warlords' civil war to gain benefits, but the unification of China has become a general demand, and it is impossible for him to use it in the end. After he bombed Zhang Zuolin to death, it promoted Zhang Xueliang's cooperation with the country. This made the majority of the Japanese people and a small number of financial groups hate Tanaka. In this year, Tanaka committed suicide. In the next few years, government leaders such as Hamaguchi and Inukai successively stabbed, and even last year's bomb case in Hongkou Park. The clues in the middle are very noteworthy.

Today's political turmoil in Japan, the rise of left-leaning thought, the increasing dissatisfaction of the proletariat and the intellectual class with the current government, and the increase in assassinations, I am afraid that the end began with the cannon of May 3rd? (To be continued)

Educational News Highlights

The Ministry of Education Solicits Opinions on Compiling Primary and Secondary School Textbooks

(Nanjing, 13th) In order to compile primary and secondary school textbooks, the Ministry of Education has ordered various departments and bureaus to collect various teaching materials compiled by local primary school teachers, and to convene primary education researchers to discuss and open up opinions on compiling primary school textbooks, and submit them to the Ministry for reference within three weeks.

The Chinese Statistical Society Holds Annual Meeting

(Nanjing, 13th) The Chinese Statistical Society held its third annual meeting on the 13th. Wang Luyi, President of the College of Political Science and Statistics, Wang Shijie, Minister of Education, and Wu Dajun, Director of the Central Statistical Office, gave speeches successively, discussing the relationship between statistics and society, politics, economy, and scientific construction. Wang Zhongwu and others were elected as the fourth session of standing committee members.

Instructions from the Jiangsu Education Department Regarding Opposition to Graduation Examinations

Zhou Fohai, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department, recently received a secret report stating that students from twelve schools, including Wuxi Normal School, held their first joint meeting at the Wuxi Education Association on May 2nd. They opposed the graduation examinations and submitted meeting minutes. Director Zhou believed that the students' excuse that the curriculum standards were not yet unified was completely unreasonable and unacceptable. He suspected that such actions were initiated by a few troublemakers and that students with good grades would not be afraid of the difficulty and would participate in the examinations. However, upon reviewing the meeting minutes, he found phrases such as "contacting various schools, uniting together, contacting by region, and electing representatives," indicating an intention to escalate the situation and potentially incite others. He instructed each school to strictly prevent and earnestly advise students not to be incited by such individuals and drawn into the vortex. Those who do not participate in the graduation examinations will not have their graduation qualifications recognized, will not be issued graduation certificates, and will not have the opportunity to further their education. In addition to instructing the Wuxi County Education Bureau to circulate this order to all public and private senior middle schools under its jurisdiction for compliance, he also instructed education bureaus in other counties to actively prepare. For those traveling long distances to take the examinations, he has already submitted a request to the Ministry of Education to consult with the Ministry of Railways to implement group ticket discounts on the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou, Tianjin-Pukou, and Longhai railway lines. If taking long-distance buses or inland river steamers, the travel will be free of charge.

Guangdong Central Petition Delegation Arrives in Shanghai

▲Most Students Have Not Yet Resumed Classes

▲Departing for Nanjing Tonight to Petition the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education

Since the Guangdong Central University incident occurred, the student body recently organized a petition delegation to go to Nanjing to petition the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education. They arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday. Most of the students at the university have still not resumed classes and are waiting for the central government to resolve the matter.

Zhong Gongxun, Li Zaixing, Rao Yuancang, and other representatives of the Sun Yat-sen University Student Association went to the Ministry of Education again at 4:00 PM on the 12th to petition. Secretary Zhou received them on behalf of the Minister. The representatives explained that the turmoil at Sun Yat-sen University had not subsided and that the students had not resumed classes for a long time, which was a great sacrifice. They requested that officials be sent to investigate the matter impartially. Zhou replied that unless Vice Minister Duan directly inquired with President Zou, it would be difficult to obtain the truth, and he promised to forward the matter to the Minister for handling. On the 12th, the association sent a telegram to all professors and students of Sun Yat-sen University, stating that they had learned of the insult and assault on professors by the medical staff at the university. They had initially hoped that the authorities would take decisive action to severely punish the perpetrators and pacify the situation, but they had received reports that the authorities were not only failing to do so but were also trying every means to protect them and place them above the law. The students, striving for justice, were also being falsely accused and arbitrarily dismissed, harming the youth more than anything else. The association expressed deep concern and felt compelled to speak out. Therefore, in addition to contacting students in Nanjing and Shanghai for unified support, they sent a telegram of condolence, urging them to continue fighting for the country and the school, and promising to provide unwavering support from afar.

Sports

Zhong Yongsen's Moving Performance Ensures China Retains the Sino-Portuguese Cup

Yesterday's Match Result: China Wins 3-2

Portuguese Team Leads 1-0 in the First Half; China Wins 3-1 in the Second Half

The Sino-Portuguese International Football Cup began in 1925, with the Chinese team winning the first championship and retaining the cup. In the following year, China and Portugal each won once, but the final match was suspended due to an incident, leaving the matter unresolved. Due to various reasons, the competition was not held for several years. This year, the leaders of the football communities of both countries revived the old event, and the Sino-Portuguese Cup, which had been interrupted, was revived. In the first match of this year, China won 7-2. Yesterday, the two countries met for the second time at the baseball field, and China won again with a score of 3-2. Thus, the Sino-Portuguese Cup was once again retained by China for another year.

▲Zhong Yongsen's Contribution Tops the Entire Team

Yesterday's victory for China was the result of the joint efforts of the entire team. However, Zhong Yongsen's contribution surpassed all others. Zhong possesses both intelligence and courage, and his skills in passing and shooting are excellent. The team's three goals, both directly and indirectly, relied on his efforts. Lu Zhongen's clean hands and feet, taking care of both high and low balls, were commendable. The reunion of Feng Yunyou and Li Ning, old partners, was also remarkable. Chen Zhenhe's experience, Tu Kaiyuan's bravery, and Liang Shutang's strength formed a solid defensive line that could rival the opponents. It is a pity that their cooperation was not yet fully refined. The three midfielders, though selected from the best, did not fully exert their strength. Avoiding rashness, they were almost smooth. Their wonderful performance and refreshing footwork were rarely seen. Wan Xianghua's several through balls were commendable.

▲Gu Sitan's Frankness is Admirable

The Portuguese team's players, possessing both strength and flexibility, were indeed formidable opponents for China. The entire team was scattered in various locations, with no possibility of coordination. Unexpectedly, once formed, they were formidable. Gu Sitan, the center-back, held a key position, leading the troops and generals, distributing their efforts, or cooperating with internal officials, guarding key points. This man truly held the key to the Portuguese team's ability to demonstrate its strength. Langgeer's agility was comparable to that of Japanese player Ke Lasha. Masail, not wearing football shoes, was inevitably inferior. The entire team performed well in the first half against the wind, but performed worse in the second half, mainly due to insufficient stamina.

▲Lu Zhongen Saves Adu Three Times

When 3:00 PM arrived, fans were still streaming in, like the waters of a river bursting its banks. He Chunhui brought the ball onto the field. With a whistle, the Portuguese team kicked off against the wind. Ke Lasha passed to Langgeer, but Feng Yunyou intercepted halfway. Wan's counterattack was unsuccessful. Gu Sitan made a long pass, and Xi Na released his horse in the suburbs. Doctor Tu could not stop him, and the ball was passed into the center. Ke Lasha shot at the goal on the penalty line, but Lu Zhongen calmly caught it and then sent it out. Leimidi entered the encirclement again. S Natuo rushed in a few steps and had a chance to shoot, but Lu Zhongen saved it again. When Xi Na came again, Lu was prepared and caught it smoothly.

▲Sun Jinshun Eager to Serve the Country

China, under heavy pressure for a long time, was eager to take action. Suddenly, Liang Shutang obtained the ball and passed it to Wan nearby. He dribbled it for two zhang and passed it to Sun Jinshun. Waiting for Gu Sitan to come and steal, the ball scurried into the east. Zhong Yongsen, like fire and boiling water, broke through three lines of defense in a row. Jiangshan'er could not resist and had to force a corner kick. Zhong kicked it in, as if writing a beginner's guide. Keluosi panicked and fouled another corner kick. Wan took the kick, which was also excellent. Doctor Tu kicked too hard, sending it into the clouds. Soon after, the Chinese flag was flying again in the Portuguese team's defense. Li Yichen, troubled by Gu Sitan, passed it urgently to Sun. He was less than ten yards from the goal. Sun Iron Leg raised his iron leg and shot with all his might, but it was five inches above the goal and lightly flew over. The audience could not help but sigh and die of regret.

▲Langgeer Builds Merit First

After this, the Chinese defense suffered frequent disasters, and dangers were often seen. B Gong Shanfu was extremely fierce, and he drilled in whenever he found an opening. Feng Yunyou lost his concentration slightly, and he went deep alone. Li Ning quickly led his troops to support him, and he kicked and shot. Lu's eyes were sharp and his feet were fast, saving the siege. China launched a counter-offensive, but was blocked and turned back. Kelasha's momentum was great, and he approached the restricted area again. Lu Zhongen was diligent and cautious, picking up the ball whenever he saw it, without any mistakes. Wan had a corner kick opportunity, which was bounced out by A Kelasha's back. Wan was still unwilling and came to attack again. Zhong Yongsen was impatient and fast, and the offside was cancelled. The Portuguese team took advantage of the emptiness of China's internal defense, and Kelasha led his troops deep. Langgeer got the ball and broke into the penalty area. Li and Feng were unable to return in time, and Langgeer shot low at the goal with a thunderous speed, and Lu Zhongen was caught off guard, and the record was opened.

▲Li Yichen Met the Opportunity

The Chinese team attacked several times, Li Yichen failed in front, and Sun Jinshun missed in the back. Doctor Tu kicked a long shot, with full force, but it was only one foot higher, and the good time in the first half passed away. The break was not long, and the warhorses were roaring again. China was in the north, facing the sun against the wind, and the situation was extremely unfavorable. At this point, the audience also said that China would hardly escape this time, but after the kick-off, the momentum was even stronger than in the first half. After three passes and two passes, Zhong had already entered the heavy defense, and was blocked by the internal guards. He quickly passed it to Wan from afar, and Wan raised his foot and flicked it back. Li Yichen was right next to the goal, and headed it in.

▲Three to Two, China Succeeds

After the autumn colors were evenly divided, the Chinese team's arrogance was even greater. Zhong Yongsen was a rare talent who came later, and his killing skills were extremely powerful, sometimes in and sometimes out, as if he was in a no-man's land. Even Yonghan such as Gu Sitan and the old hero Mai Sail could not do anything to him. At one point, Zhong was injured by a collision and left the field. Not long after, he returned to the field from the inside to help the war. The Chinese team's forwards increased their courage a lot. In an instant, Zhong's arrogance swallowed up the mountains and rivers, and he was alone in the battle, avoiding tens of thousands of people, carrying the ball straight in, and smashing into the dragon gate, taking the lead with two to one, winning the sound of applause. China turned defeat into victory and continued to attack. The Portuguese were not willing to be slaughtered and took the opportunity to retaliate. Therefore, the Chinese defense was not consolidated, the wind was strong and the ball was fast, and Chen Zhenhe's interception failed. B Gong Shanfu took the lead, fifteen yards from the near door, with a bang, and the game was tied again. At this point, the atmosphere of the war became tense again. Zhong Yongsen launched an uprising on the border, as fast as flying, and the next Nato lost his horse, and Mai Sail came to chase him very hard. Zhong had no one in his eyes, until the penalty line, he hurriedly sent it to the front of the door. Li Yichen could not shoot, and Wan's feet swayed across. General Zhong returned to the battlefield, and swept his body, and the ball entered the door. The four seats cheered wildly. Although the Portuguese tried hard to counterattack, but the time did not allow, a whistle, and my China won the championship calmly.

Jiangda Games Day Two

Today, the All-Around Sports Athletics Championships Will Be Resolved

Field Event Championship Belongs to National Central University with 36 Points

Track Event Championship Belongs to Guanghua University with 35 Points

Hu Ruisheng Equals National Record in Women's 100 Meters

A Total of Ten New Records Were Set During the Two Days of the Meet

The sixth Jiangda University Track and Field Meet has concluded yesterday. Starting today, the all-around events will begin, and the women's track and field events will also conclude today. National Central University won the championship with 36 points. In the track events championship, National Central University and Guanghua University had equal scores throughout, creating a tense situation. It was not until the final 800-meter race that Guanghua took a two-point lead and won the championship with 35 points. National Central University came in second with 33. In terms of men's and women's results, a total of nine new records were set, and Ms. Hu Ruisheng equaled Sun Guiyun's national record of 13.4 seconds in the 100-meter dash, which is commendable. Details are as follows:

A Glimpse of the Venue

Yesterday, the wind became stronger, and felt hats and straw hats were blown all over the venue, making the competition more difficult. Because all the events were finals, and the track and field championships were yet to be decided, the audience was twice as large as on the first day, with many women also in attendance. The track competition between Guanghua and National Central University was particularly fierce. As a result, Guanghua won the championship with 35 points to 32. Guanghua students were excited and cheered incessantly. National Central University was victorious in the field events and women's sports, and their cheers often battled with those of Guanghua, adding much to the excitement of the venue.

Views on Success and Failure

▲Guanghua Has Outstanding Talent in Track Events

▲National Central University Lacks Outstanding Talent

▲Daxia's Field Events Are Flawed

The men's track and field championship has been decided, with the field events going to National Central University and the track events going to Guanghua, marking the first time Guanghua has won the Jiangda University track and field championship. The reason why National Central University won against Daxia in the field events is that they have more talent and are more well-rounded. Daxia lacked talent in the pole vault and triple jump, how could they hope to win? In the track events, Guanghua won first place in six of the eight events, which is commendable. The reason for National Central University's failure can be summarized in one sentence: although they have many talented people, they lack outstanding individuals, so in the final 800-meter race to decide the outcome, they could only listen to their natural failure.

Field Event Results

▲Shot Put Final was Fierce

▲Yang and Chen Both Set New Records

▲Women's High Jump also Set New Record

Yesterday's field events included four men's events. The Shot Put was the most fierce competition. Yang Yongcan of National Central University and Chen Baoqiu of Daxia both set new meet records with 12.20 meters. National Central University had a wealth of talent in the Pole Vault, sweeping the top three places. The champion, Li Disheng, had a profound understanding of the sport, with graceful posture and skill of 3.37 meters, which was not easy. If there had been no strong winds, the results could have been even better. Zhou Mengqiao's triple jump of 12.27 meters was also rare. Although the Javelin final was with the wind, the results were mediocre. The famous Wang Jihuai only took first place with 42.95 meters, which was unexpected. The women's field events included two events. Wu Houbai took first place in the Shot Put with 7.80 meters, and Ms. Hu Ruisheng set a new meet record in the High Jump with 1.20 meters. Details are described below.

▲Men's Shot Put The two veterans Chen Baoqiu (Daxia) and Yang Yongcan (National Central University) competed extremely fiercely. Chen first reached a distance of 11.20 meters, marking it with a small pennant. Yang Yongcan used his brute strength, and several times in a row, he was finally caught up. However, the ball thrown by Yang hit Chen's flag, making it difficult to measure Yang's distance. A certain referee who inserted the pole at the time inserted Yang's flag near Chen's, leaving a distance of an inch or so. National Central University believed that this was incorrect, and reported it to Chief Referee Shen Siliang. Shen also believed that it was difficult to distinguish who was closer, so he assumed that the distance between the two was equal, and exceptionally Chen and Yang had another three final throws. Whoever threw the farthest would get first place. Chen Baoqiu threw first, and both times were farther than Yang Yongcan. Who knew that in the last time, Yang used all his strength and threw with all his might, actually exceeding Chen's mark. After measuring, Yang's farthest was 10.94 meters, and Chen's was 10.75 meters. Thus, the first place in the shot put went to Yang Yongcan, and Chen was the runner-up. However, the results were the same, both being 11.20 meters, breaking Lu Ming's Jiangda record of 10.73 meters.

Track Event Sketches

(1) 100 Meters

▲ Chen Jiayou Leans Forward to Win: The 100-meter race was the first final in the men's track events and one of the most exciting. Short-distance heroes gathered on the line. Due to a slight wind, the starter consulted with the athletes, ordering them to run backward from the finish line. Everyone was unwilling, so the record was counted as being with the wind. On the first start, Huang Feilong of Jinan, who had achieved a time of 11.2 seconds the day before, false-started. On the second restart, Huang could not avoid feeling disheartened, leading to him falling behind. For the first 40 meters, the seven runners advanced almost in a line, making it difficult to distinguish who was in the lead. After 50 meters, Wang Jihuai led by two feet. Chen Jiayou of Jinan chased hard behind Wang. Approaching the finish line, they arrived almost simultaneously. However, Chen Jiayou leaned his chest forward, securing first place. Wang was second, Xu in third was also very close, and Lu Linyu in fourth was slightly behind. Huang Feilong was fifth, with a time of 11.4 seconds, tying the Jiangda record.

(2) 200 Meters

▲ Wang Jihuai Strives for Revenge: Wang Jihuai, having only lost by a hair's breadth in the 100 meters, was determined to win the 200 meters. Eight runners started. Chen Jiayou, after the 100-meter high hurdles, lacked the strength. At 80 meters after the start of the 200 meters, his momentum waned, and he withdrew. The remaining seven continued forward. Initially, it was difficult to tell who was in the lead. At the 100-meter mark, Wang Jihuai held a significant advantage, leading by two feet. Xu Biao from Central chased hard behind. Arriving at the finish line, the difference between Xu and Wang was truly no more than a shoulder's width. It was indeed a close call. Ma Yu was third, and Huang Feilong was fourth, with a time of 24.1 seconds, breaking the Jiangda record.

(3) 400 Meters

▲ Dong Shuzhao Shows His Power Again: Dong Shuzhao, having already won the 1500 meters, displayed great power in the 400 meters, leading all the way. The other runners were no match for him. He finished more than four meters ahead of the second-place finisher. The time of 54 and four-fifths seconds can be said to be not bad. Second place was Liu Fukang from Jiaotong. Tao Yingjie from Guanghua was more than four meters behind Liu, an unexpected result. Ma Yu from Central finished fourth.

(4) 800 Meters

▲ The Championship Hinges on This Event: The final determination of the track championship between Guanghua and Central depended entirely on this event. On the first day, they each scored five points. In the 100 meters, they each scored three points. In the 200 meters, they each scored five points. In the 400 meters, Guanghua exceeded by six points. Central regained seven points in the high hurdles, leading by one point. After the 10,000 meters, the two schools were equal again. The decision of the championship hinged entirely on the very last 800 meters. Guanghua had two runners, and Central had three. In the first lap, Hu Shixuan remained in the lead. Dong Shuzhao was not flustered, steadily following. The third and fourth runners were also from Central, followed by Liu Fukang from Jiaotong. Dong was five hundred meters behind Hu. In the final 250 meters, Dong Shuzhao began to sprint, charging forward like a runaway horse. At the finish line, Hu was twenty meters behind Dong. Hu was exhausted, and Liu Fukang from Jiaotong made a push to overtake him at the line. Hu finished third, and Tian Hanlin from Central finished fourth, with a very good time of 2 minutes 11 seconds, breaking the Jiangda record. The track championship thus went to Guanghua.

(5) 10,000 Meters

▲ Liu Chongli Runs Further and Further Ahead: Liu Chongli's victory in the 10,000 meters for Guanghua did not involve intense competition. After 4,000 meters, there was no room for competition. Peng Shuxin led at the start, followed by Liu, then Zhou Guangwu from Jinan and Jiang Wensen from Central. Zhou Guangwu was tall with long strides, running very fast. For the first 2,000 meters, Zhou was clearly in first place, with Liu following. Zhou gradually slowed down, looking tired. Reaching 4,000 meters, Liu Chongli surged ahead. Zhou Guangwu fell to second, followed by Jiang Wensen, Su Keming, Peng Shuxin, Bao Heqing, and Zhan Yiji in order. Reaching 6,000 meters, Liu ran further and further ahead, and Zhou Guangwu was overtaken by Jiang Wensen, with Zhou in second. Su Keming, Bao Heqing, and Zhan Yiji followed. At 7,000 meters and 8,000 meters, Zhou Guangwu fell further and further behind. Jiang Wensen, Peng Shuxin, and Bao Heqing advanced in that order, with Zhan Yiji chasing Zhou in sixth. Liu Chongli reached the finish line, with Jiang Wensen 400 meters behind, Peng Shuxin another 400 meters behind, and Bao Heqing in fourth. Zhou Guangwu was fifth, and Zhan Yiji was sixth, with an average time of 39 minutes, 25 and four-fifths seconds.

(6) High Hurdles

▲ Liu Yingjun's Graceful Form: With only five runners starting, Liu Yingjun had the fastest start and the most graceful form over the hurdles. Chen Jiayu chased desperately behind, very close over the last hurdle. However, Chen jumped too high over the hurdle, slowing his advance, and Liu reached the finish line. Chen was second, Xu Rukang third, and Chen Hongqi fourth, with a time of 17.1 seconds, breaking the Jiangda record.

200 Meters Ties Sun Guiyun's Record and Hu Ruisheng's First Place in the High Jump (Photos by Sun Qichang and Ma Xiezong)

(7) Intermediate Hurdles

▲ Tao Yingjie's Specialty: Tao Yingjie gave up the high hurdles to focus on the intermediate hurdles, easily defeating Zhu Shouhun from Central. He led all the way, as the intermediate hurdles were Tao's specialty. However, due to a lack of practice, the time was not good, 64 and three-fifths seconds. Zhu was second, Liu Yingjun third, and Wang Fengting from Jinling fourth.

(8) Women's 50 Meters

▲ Hu Ruisheng Unbeatable: This was a preliminary round, divided into two groups. There was wind. Hu Ruisheng was unbeatable in the first group, finishing three meters ahead of Liu Guanglin. The time of 7.4 seconds was counted as being with the wind, but was still excellent. In the second group, (1), (2), and (3) were very close, with Zhou Yueying first at 7.5 seconds. In today's final, Hu Ruisheng secured first place.

The Four Track Stars of Guanghua (From right to left): Tao Yingjie, Wang Jihuai, Dong Shuzhao, Liu Chongli (Photo by Li Zunyong)

(9) Women's 100 Meters

▲ Ties Sun Guiyun's Record: Due to the small number of participants, it was changed to a final. Hu Ruisheng created a surprising record of 13.8 seconds, tying Sun Guiyun's record, with quick strides and excellent form. Zhou Yueying was second, far behind.

(10) Women's 200 Meters

▲ Central Sweeps Again: The women's events were entirely swept by female students from Central, including in the 200 meters: (1) Guo Zongying, (2) Chen Qing, (3) Wu Houbai. Cao Huizhen from Guanghua finished fourth, with an average time of 33.4 seconds.
