Free Talk

Plan

— Shi Yi

Since the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan achieved results, the term "plan" has become very popular, such as the Hoover Twenty-Year Plan and the Hitler Four-Year Plan, etc. All the tunes are sung very nicely. However, the former ended with Hoover losing his job as president before the plan could be fully realized, and Hitler has only just started. Apart from excluding Jews and arresting communists, there hasn't been much significant progress yet. In China, whatever the world has, we must also have it, so there is a certain minister's Four-Year Industrial Construction Plan. As for whether this plan has already started and how it is progressing, forgive me for not being able to or having the right to investigate, so I dare not make hasty judgments. What I want to talk about is another kind of plan.

This is what the big headline in the recent newspapers told me:

"Enemy troops in eastern Luan are advancing steadily, and our troops plan to retreat westward." Please allow me to add a little commentary. The word "plan" here is used as an adverbial adjective, meaning "in a planned manner," not as a verb still "in the planning" stage. Originally, we had known for a long time about the news that "our troops have safely withdrawn!" The ability to "withdraw" and do so "safely" naturally implies a pre-existing plan.

I have not read books such as Sun Tzu's "Art of War," and I am completely ignorant of modern military science. I only remember reading the "Romance of the Three Kingdoms" as a child, knowing that "make the real appear unreal, and the unreal appear real" is a common strategy used by military strategists; and military common sense such as "retreat to advance, defend to attack," and "lure the enemy deep and annihilate them in a concentrated manner" has occasionally been gleaned from war news. Therefore, I believe that a planned withdrawal is naturally aimed at a counterattack, especially since news reports also contain phrases such as "many enemies annihilated at the front," making it even more believable that this withdrawal is not a defeat. Therefore, I have always been optimistic, hoping that one day we will "recover lost territory."

However, after seeing the conversation of Mr. Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Committee, my optimism could not help but waver greatly. Mr. Wu said, "We only hope that land that can be lost in three days will take two months to lose." This is probably the "entire plan." If we follow this plan, I dare not speculate on when the entire China will be "lost"; even just thinking about the soldiers who are fighting in hand-to-hand combat under the artillery fire, and that the price of their flesh and blood is only to exchange "three days" for "two months," I don't know how to express myself.

However, as soon as I think that this is to realize the plan, I have to accept it as satisfactory.

Visit

— Lou Jinsheng

After walking for a while in the warm sunlight, I arrived at the home of the wife of my recently deceased friend, Ru. I sipped the green tea in my glass, looking at the wife of my deceased friend sitting across from me as I spoke. She is a woman who loves to move and talk. Today, she was wearing a washed-out, ill-fitting patriotic cloth shirt. Because of the heat, her face was very radiant. Ru died only last year. I haven't seen Ru's wife for three or four months. I thought she hadn't changed at all, still smiling and talking lively, making people feel that the only difference was that she was wearing a more plain cloth shirt than before.

When Ru and Yu were in love, I had also helped them. When they were pursuing this matter, I even jokingly said to Ru, "Sometimes I also love Yu," which made Ru unhappy. Now, facing the young woman in front of me, this woman wearing a washed-out, ill-fitting patriotic cloth shirt, and thinking that she is already a "widow," some restless thoughts naturally arose. But then I thought of my deceased friend, our friendship which was not superficial, and some remorse surfaced in my heart. I hurriedly searched for an irrelevant sentence to cover up my unease:

"Do you know how Liu Yuzhen is doing now?"

"I don't know... I don't correspond with anyone now. Let those who know that Ru is dead know, and I won't write letters to those who don't."

Liu Yuzhen was a friend who was often with Ru and Yu when they were in love, and now she is a woman who is married and has children. When Yu said that she doesn't correspond with anyone now, the face that was originally smiling suddenly showed a heavy shadow, and her tone became hard. Then, I saw two lines of clear tears streaming down her eyes.

"What's wrong? Are you so discouraged?"

I felt that I was too clumsy and said such a thing. I regretted it, I shouldn't have stirred up her pain, and I was too young to give her some gentle comfort, so I had to sit quietly with apology. Fortunately, this period of silence did not last long, and she had already put on a cheerful face. She didn't want to let people know her pain. I knew it.

Confused thoughts made it impossible for me to stay here any longer. I just said, "I'll come see you again when I have time," and left. But on the way, the melancholy in my heart was truly unknown to anyone!

Below the Dantian

— Jian Guang

Mr. Cao Juren said: Enlightened people practice guidance and supplementation, returning to the Dantian. The method is skillful and the time is slow. For example: a fox from the Republic of China in the years 12 and 13, practicing Taoism in Beijing. It wasn't until this year that both chickens and dogs became immortals. Taking ten years is too long. As far as I know, modern Taoist priests have their own electric cultivation methods, not returning to the "Dantian" but returning to below the "Dantian."

Cultivation below the "Dantian" includes the art of the bedroom and the "Classic of the Plain Girl." The Yellow Emperor ascended to immortality after having intercourse with seventy-seven forty-nine women, and the wonders below the "Dantian" are even more indescribable. If Mr. Ye Dehui heard my statement, he would surely laugh loudly in the underworld and say, "My Dao is not alone!"

Let me illustrate with an example. Yang Taizhen's unofficial biography states: "In the seventh month of the fourth year of Tianbao, the Yang family was made a noble concubine, her father Xuan Yan was given the title of Prefect of Jiyin, her mother, Li, was made Lady of Longxi Commandery, and her cousin Zhao was appointed as a minister. In the seventh year, Zhao was promoted to Imperial Censor and given the title of Prefect of the Capital, and given the name Guozhong. Her eldest sister was made Lady of Han, her third sister was made Lady of Guo, and her eighth sister was made Lady of Qin; they all received their orders on the same day, and each received 100,000 coins per month for cosmetics." The crystallization of our country's spiritual civilization, where chickens and dogs become immortals through methods below the Dantian, is another secret of Taoist practice. Mr. Cao Juren's thinking is old-fashioned, only seeing the wonderful use of the "Dantian"; but not knowing the wonderful use of "below the Dantian," which has existed since ancient times and is prevalent today, and must be praised!

There is a character in the Grand View Garden, who has no connection with the Jia family, but comes to live in the Grand View Garden because of cultivating the "Dantian." Mr. Cao Xueqin's veiled writing seems to tell us that the reason she wins the favor of the Jia family is also "below the Dantian." That person is Miaoyu, and everyone should respect her!

A Tang Dynasty folk song says: "Don't be sad when giving birth to a daughter, don't be happy when giving birth to a son!" This can be used as a praise for today!

Amao

— Zhu Xun Yuan

The cold wind seeped in through the cracks in the door, and the bean-like lamplight flickered uncertainly. Everything around was quiet. Amao was staring blankly at the lamplight, pondering his fate.

Amao, everyone in the village knew him as a frugal man, who didn't gamble or smoke. But in recent years, he didn't know what kind of bad luck he'd encountered, not only selling off the several acres of land passed down from his ancestors, but also incurring a lot of debt.

The year before last, the water was high, and Amao's fields were flooded. Half a year of hard work only yielded a few grains of rice. The money he exchanged was not enough to pay the rent rice to Master Wang in the city. So he had to borrow dozens of yuan from Master Gu in the town. After several bitter pleas, he finally borrowed fifty yuan. It was stated that the monthly interest was 2.5%; this 2.5% monthly interest was still Master Gu seeing that he was pitiful and taking pity on him.

Last autumn, the weather was really good, and the rice grew green and tall. After Amao ate dinner, he always went to the head of the field every day to take a walk, looking at the plump rice ears, a kind of inexplicable joy would slip out from his heart. He would laugh in his heart. The rice gently swayed in the evening breeze, as if laughing with him. Lying in bed at night, although he felt a little sore in his bones, the golden hope made him forget the hard work of the day.

When the rice was brought to the threshing ground, the price of rice fell, and Amao's hope was shattered.

Amao sold all the rice, earning a total of more than a hundred yuan. He paid off Master Gu's debt, paid half of the bean cake money he owed, and there were still two old silver dollars hiding in Amao's pocket, and a few liters of coarse rice piled in the rice bucket at home.

On the tenth day of the tenth month, Master Wang in the city opened his granary. Amao's neighbor, Ashui, had already collected dozens of yuan to pay it back, and Uncle Zhang and Li Genbao had also gone to the city to pay it back. The rest of the villagers were delaying, and Amao was of course one of them.

The third deadline (Note 1) had passed, and Uncle (Note 2) had come to urge him

Carrot Top

— Jules Renard, translated by Lin Qu

Kettle (continued)

Mrs. Lepic: Look at that puddle of mud dripping down from the fireplace, Eulalie. Now that’s a fine mess. Eulalie, why was my kettle stolen without anyone telling me? Perhaps you took it?

Mrs. Lepic: This kettle belongs to this family, Eulalie. Am I, Mr. Lepic, or my children supposed to ask your permission whenever we need to use it?

Eulalie: When I get really angry, I say stupid things.

Mrs. Lepic: Are you angry at us, or at yourself, Eulalie? Yes, who are you angry at, anyway? Although I’m not really curious, I’d really like to know. You’re really putting me in a bind. You use the excuse that the kettle is missing, and you unhesitatingly pour a bucket of water on the fire, refusing to admit your own mistake, and blaming others, even me. I think I haven’t said anything wrong!

Eulalie: Carrot Top, my darling, do you know where my kettle is?

Mrs. Lepic: How would he know? He’s just a child who doesn’t take care of anything. Let’s not talk about your kettle anymore. I think you’d better think about what you said yesterday: "Once I find that I can’t even boil a kettle of water myself, I’ll get out of here immediately, without anyone having to push me." True, I think there’s something wrong with your eyes, but I didn’t expect it to reach the point of despair. I won't say anything else, Eulalie, just please put yourself in my shoes. You understand the situation as clearly as I do; please think carefully and draw a conclusion. Ah! Please don’t hold back anything, just cry as much as you want. It's worth crying over.

Words Unspoken

“Mama! Eulalie!”

……………………

What else did he want to say, Carrot Top? He would have made everything worse. Fortunately, under Mrs. Lepic’s cold gaze, he suddenly stopped.

Why say to Eulalie:

“I took it, Eulalie!”

Nothing could save the old woman. Her eyes couldn’t see clearly anymore, her eyes couldn’t see clearly anymore. Never mind her. She would have to give in sooner or later. Carrot Top's confession would only have made her even more upset. It's better to let her go, better to let her not suspect Carrot Top at all, and just think that she was struck by an unavoidable fate.

And why say to Mrs. Lepic:

“Mama, I took it!”

Why take credit even if you did something praiseworthy? Why must you beg for a rewarding smile? Not only is there no benefit to this, but it is also dangerous, because he knows that Mrs. Lepic will scold him in public, so it is better to help her to the end, a better way is to pretend to help his mother and Eulalie find the kettle.

When the three of them worked together to find the kettle, he seemed the most enthusiastic.

Mrs. Lepic seemed to think it was none of her business and was the first to give up.

Eulalie endured and ran away, muttering in her mouth. Because of his caution, Carrot Top, who almost ruined things, also put away his strength, like a tool that was no longer needed.

Spring and Autumn

Novel and Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals

— Zhan Lu

Someone asked me how to write a novel. It happened that I had a copy of Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals stacked on my desk, and I said with a smile: "This is the encyclopedia of novels. Reading one volume of Zuo's Commentary is better than reading a hundred novels by famous authors."

People suspected that I was joking, but I pointed out many pieces of evidence from Zuo in a serious manner:

Zuo's Commentary is detailed in military strategies and tactics, so it is a military novel. It is detailed in social shortcomings, so it is a social novel. Moreover, this blind Mr. Zuo Qiuming is the most gifted in writing about emotions; Wu Chen eloping with a woman and Xu Mei supporting her husband are romance novels. Ai Jiang crying and calling to the heavens in the marketplace is a tragic novel. Ji Qian refusing to marry and Zhong Jian betraying me are chivalrous novels. Two sons throwing themselves into the river and Lady Shi making a vow are melodrama novels. The New Terrace giving rise to slander and Ai Jia composing a song are scandal novels. Zhongzi's hand pattern and Yan Ji's orchid omen are bizarre novels.

Furthermore, the crows in the Chu tent and the joy in the mulberry tree are detective novels. Ge Lu knowing the language of cows and Shi Kuang recognizing the south wind are science fiction novels. Zheng Qiao discussing souls and Yan Zi distinguishing harmony and sameness are philosophical novels. Ying Kao Shu leaving soup for his mother and Jin Ling Zhe thinking of his mother are ethical novels. The stone speaking in the state of Jin and the snakes fighting at the Zheng gate are supernatural novels. Dwarfs being defeated by Zhu and Yu En abandoning his armor are humorous novels. Other things, other things, countless other things, I will not say anymore.

This is me compiling a table of contents for Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals, and it is also me advertising Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals; most young people like to read novels but do not like to read Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals, thinking that Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals is dull; in fact, how is it dull? Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals is a good novel that is all-encompassing.

I wrote this article in the "Spring and Autumn" column precisely to arouse the readers' interest in Zuo's Commentary on the Spring and Autumn Annals.

The Great Way Society

— Fu Yizhi

In the border region of Jiangxi and Fujian, in the past two years, due to the ravages of the Fang-Shao bandit gangs, the people have been in dire straits. The so-called Great Way Society, which recites incantations and eats talismans to resist bullets, has emerged in response to this situation. This society's influence is not great, and people in distant places may not know about it, so I am introducing it here, with the intention of simply making some random remarks.

According to a man from Shangrao in Jiangxi: the leader of this society uses the recitation of incantations and the eating of talismans to resist bullets as a slogan. There is a branch in Tieshan, Shangrao. At first, there were only ten or twenty people, but then the society performed Taoist magic, which indeed had aspects that could make people deeply believe. As a result, people continued to request to join, and it became an anti-Communist organization. When joining the society as a member for the first time, a certain amount of membership fee must be paid, and then Taoist magic is taught. Every time they fought with small groups of local bandits, they first had each member recite incantations, draw talismans, and drink them down. Another talisman was attached to the abdominal wall. The weapons they held were purely large knives, spears, and so on, so the locals mistakenly called them the Big Knife Society.

The members of the society believed that bullets could not harm them, and whenever the Communists came to attack, they all rushed to meet the enemy. Each time they won, the locals became even more convinced. Recently, the society engaged in a fierce battle with a bandit gang in the Huating area of Shangrao, and they captured more than twenty rifles and several boxes of bullets. Guo Su, the county magistrate of Shangrao, heard about this and awarded them twenty rifles, saying that although the society was somewhat superstitious, it was commendable that they could capture firearms, and their bravery was also commendable.

Whether the society uses magic to deceive people or not, it can use superstitious psychology to inspire the masses to resist the Communists, which is not comparable to the Miao and Yao people who use "Revive the Miao and Destroy the Han" as a slogan. Therefore, I am happy to introduce it here.

Impressions of Linggu Temple

— Zhen

The mountains of Jinling, generally speaking, are mostly majestic but not graceful, steep but not secluded; bare and barren, giving people a not very good impression. But the scenery of Linggu Temple cannot be considered an exception. This place is only one or two li away from the Zhongshan Mausoleum, and it is located on the eastern foothills of Zhongshan Mountain, with deep bamboo groves and dense forests, and winding paths leading to secluded places. Looking from afar, an ancient temple is surrounded by thousands of peaks piercing the sky and ten thousand pines forming waves, resembling a natural landscape painting; the atmosphere is ever-changing, leisurely and silent, making people can't help but yearn for it!

Now, with spring turning to summer, a person placing himself in this rare environment will not only have a refreshed perspective, but also smell the fragrance of wild grass and idle flowers, which will make his mind feel free and happy! Although there are not many peonies and peonies in Linggu Temple, they have caused a sensation among the people of the capital, and on weekends and holidays, people take the mausoleum tour buses to Linggu Temple at lightning speed; making the Confucius Temple and Xuanwu Lake lose their luster!

This Linggu Temple, some people compare it to the Longhua Temple in Shanghai, and others say that it is similar to the Zhaoyin Temple in Zhenjiang. But I think that only the Lian Temple on the shore of West Lake in Hangzhou can be compared. As for the famous Lingyin Temple, it may even be inferior!

Behind the temple is the Baogong Pagoda, which is said to be the location where the bones of Zhi Gong are buried. It is now being completely rebuilt and renovated, and the majestic nine-story pagoda will become the tallest steel-concrete stone pagoda in Jiangnan; the project has been underway for two years, and it is already quite impressive.

It is said that there is a stone tablet there, on which is painted an image of Zhi Gong, which is the handwriting of Wu Daozi, and there is also an inscription made by Li Taibai; and Yan Lugong personally wrote the title; collectively known as the "Three Perfections Tablet". Recently, when many of us went to visit, we never saw it. I don't know where it has gone?

I Want to Study Veterinary Medicine

— Dingming

Veterinary medicine is an official title. It belongs to the Tianshi of the Zhou Rites and is in charge of treating animal diseases and sores. Now, all countries have veterinary medicine specialties; like the veterinary school attached to the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center. But in civilized, progressive, and scientifically developed countries, they not only promote the health of their people's bodies and minds, but also promote the health of animals; what about our China? Last year, there was a large outbreak of cholera and bubonic plague in Shaanxi; not to mention other things.

The countryside is full of sick chickens, sick dogs, sick pigs, sick cattle, sick sheep, and black sheep; recently, I wanted to study veterinary medicine; if I become a veterinary expert, I will go back to the countryside and treat them in a practical way; to make them change their beastly hearts and become trustworthy, loyal, things that can be loaded with things, and meritorious ox brothers, the Lamb of God.

If (again, if) my goal is achieved, then I will further study to become a hunter; I do not hope to chase the deer in the Central Plains; but I want to shoot down the eagles, falcons, and drug lords that startle from the high sky, and the jackals, wolves, foxes, and swarms of rats that run rampant in the mountains and fields.

Learning Pills

— Yan Ye

Since the method of requiring junior and senior high school students to lightly pass the qualifying exam was stipulated, the "Essential Readings for the Qualifying Exam" have been produced in the market. The qualifying exam not only examines the last semester's coursework, but all coursework at each stage must be tested, which is recognized as a difficult hurdle for students, and the "Essential Readings for the Qualifying Exam" are naturally welcomed by them. All kinds of textbooks read over the years can be put on the shelf, just take a simplified and simplified "Essential Readings for the Qualifying Exam", and intensify your efforts to embrace the Buddha's feet temporarily day and night, and you can boldly go to the exam.

Some people say: Simplified qualifying exam books are easier to read and remember than complicated textbooks, but after all, you still have to read and remember them. It is best if our scientists can invent a kind of learning pill, take the essence of party ideology, and make party ideology pills. Take the essence of Chinese language, and make Chinese language pills. Other mathematics, history, geography, chemistry, physics, foreign languages, etc., can also be made into scientific pills. If you want to understand party ideology, you only need to buy a party ideology pill, dissolve it in boiling water and take it, and you will become a party ideology expert. If you want to understand Chinese, mathematics, English, and other subjects, you can do the same. Isn't this the most scientific method that does not require reading and memorizing? And the students will definitely buy silk and embroider the image of the inventor of these learning pills, and put this image above the portrait of our Mr. Sun Yat-sen.

That person also said: These learning pills can be divided into two types: one for each subject and one for mixed subjects. Whether it is for each subject or mixed, it can be divided into three grades: elementary school, middle school, and university. The prices of each subject pill are slightly lower. Mixed learning pills are made by mixing the essence of each subject, and by eating one pill, you will understand each subject, and one person is omnipotent, so the price can be sold high, and the three grades of large, medium, and small have their own prices.

I hope that these learning pills can be realized in the shortest period of time, because it is of immeasurable merit to people and of infinite benefit to oneself, and in the history of invention in the world, my page, although no one pays attention to it now, will become the most important page from now on.

Full-Length Novel

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 6: Cold Observation of Sweet and Bitter Love Affairs from Two Sides; Three-Year Agreement on a Rough World Path

Gui Zhi unknowingly finished eating a bowl of lotus root flour. Thinking that if she didn't speak again, the opportunity would pass, she smiled shyly at Ji Zhi. Ji Zhi smiled back when he saw her smile. Gui Zhi asked: What are you smiling at? Ji Zhi smiled and said: Whatever you smile at, I smile at. Gui Zhi blushed, picked up a piece of sponge cake from the fruit plate and looked at it, but still put it down. Ji Zhi said: If you want to eat it, just eat it, why are you being so polite? Gui Zhi shook her head and said: I don't want to eat anything. I didn't come here to eat. Ji Zhi smiled and said: You didn't come here to eat, what did you come for? As he spoke, he tilted his head and looked at Gui Zhi's face. Gui Zhi smiled and hid her head under her arm, raised it, and said seriously: I have a serious question to ask you, can't you live separately from your brother? As soon as Ji Zhi heard this, he knew there was another deeper meaning, and said: If I can be financially independent, of course I can live separately from my brother. Although my brother is very strict with me, he has brought me up from reading to now, and I can't help but obey him. Gui Zhi couldn't say anything for a long time after hearing this, holding the copper spoon for scooping lotus root flour in her hand, she kept drawing in the empty bowl. The other hand supported her half-tilted head. Although she didn't say anything, seeing her appearance, she knew that she was very unhappy. Ji Zhi smiled at her and said: What do you mean? Gui Zhi pouted and said: What do I mean? She answered Ji Zhi's words, but her eyes were looking into the empty bowl. Ji Zhi said: I understand what you mean, and I am very grateful for your kindness to me. Generally speaking, I should immediately make a pact with you and work together. But I don't have any savings on hand now. If we cooperate, I will definitely fall out with my brother, and my job will naturally be lost along with it. Then, what will I do in the future? If you believe me, please wait for me for three years. During these three years, I will definitely think of a way. However, three years is a bit too long. Are you saying that I am shirking my responsibility? (69)

Children's Paradise

The Cleverness of Birds

One day I saw a small crow. It wanted to drink the water in the bottle, but the water in the bottle was shallow and its beak was short, so it couldn't drink it at all. It stood by the mouth of the bottle, thinking and thinking, and came up with a way. It held small stones in its mouth from the ground and threw them into the bottle, so that the water in the bottle gradually rose, and then it could drink it. If children keep mountain sparrows at home, they can try to see if the water in the cage is shallow, and the mountain sparrow will definitely throw the sand shells of the food in the cage into the bottle.

Animals that Can Stand Upright

Among all wild animals, only bears can stand upright on their hind legs like humans, because the soles of the bear's hind feet are exactly the same as those of humans. Although apes can stand upright, the soles of their hind feet cannot fully touch the ground, so they cannot walk like humans. All other animals stand on the strength of their toes.

The Use of Airplanes

We need to know how many kinds of uses there are for airplanes now? Roughly speaking, the following fourteen kinds can be included. (1) Military use, (2) Fishery (detecting the location of fish schools), (3) Transporting special goods (such as fresh fish, news, letters, mail), (4) Exploration, (5) Watching over mountains and forests, (6) Searching for maritime disasters, (7) Propaganda advertisements, (8) Surveying (investigating water sources, organizing cultivated land, laying railways, etc.) (9) Rescuing lives (dropping food supplies) (10) Transporting passengers, (11) Agriculture (scattering seeds, fertilizers, insecticides) (11) Measuring meteorology, (12) Pursuing criminals, (10) Animal husbandry (using airplanes to chase livestock when they leave the fence)

Western Woman

A white cloth towel can be used to make an interesting Western woman figure, as shown in the diagram below. In the first picture, first tear open both ends of the cloth towel and make two thin sticks as shown in the figure.

In the second picture, tie a knot in the lower part of the middle to form the body, two legs, and a skirt.

In the third picture, cut open both sides of the paper above the body, pull out the middle stick to form two hands, and finally make a face, but the head and face must not be too large, and if it is too large, cut off a little.

In the fourth picture, there is still a knot to make a hat, and all the useless parts are completely cut off, and then it becomes the Western woman figure in the fifth picture.

The Donkey's Loyalty

— Chu

About thirty li outside the city of Beiping, there is a small village. There is an old man named Long in the village. One day, he rode a donkey to Beiping to go to the market. On the way, he suddenly met robbers, and the money, goods, and the donkey he was riding were all robbed by the robbers. Later, after half a year, the donkey suddenly carried a child back to the Long family, and the people in the Long family were extremely surprised. The child was only six or seven years old. The people in the Long family asked him in detail about his name and address, thinking of sending him back the next day. Unexpectedly, the child's father was the robber who had robbed Long's property. When he saw Long personally sending his son home, he was not only extremely panicked, but also extremely grateful. He returned the property he had robbed from before, doubled, and begged Long to spare his life, and swore that he would never be a robber again. Seeing his sincerity, Long did not pursue the past. As for why the donkey carried the child back to the Long family? It turned out that one day, the robber's son rode the donkey outside to play. The donkey recognized the road and thought of its former master, so it took the opportunity to carry the child back.

Silver Price Decline, Tightening of Foreign Exchange Market

Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation and Banque Belge pour l'Étranger Over-Sell Excessively

Gold Industry Settles Over Four Hundred Thousand

According to yesterday's foreign dispatch, London's spot and forward silver prices both fell by 0.0625, but the underlying demand remained good. The British pound strengthened against the U.S. dollar by 0.25, while the U.S. dollar weakened against the British pound by 0.01625. Securities: Japanese Planes Reconnoiter Peace and Tianjin

Bond Market Re-Emerges in a State of Chaos

Yesterday, the bond market at the Chinese Securities Exchange still showed signs of turmoil. Japanese planes repeatedly reconnoitered Peiping, causing anxiety among the people and creating a sense of impending doom. The defenses of Miyun were at risk, and if they were to fall, the enemy would have no obstacles. It was uncertain whether Britain and the United States would speak up righteously, but at this time they remained silent. Therefore, if the situation were to escalate, the future of the bond market would be fraught with storms. However, the general bullish sentiment was very strong, and the support was substantial. When market prices fell significantly, they would step in to support it, as evidenced by past events. In the early morning session, the initial market prices could not maintain their original levels due to the renewed reconnaissance by enemy aircraft over Peiping, which caused continued apprehension. However, as the selling pressure from the northern group subsided, the market prices only fell by a small amount, ranging from 0.1 to 0.3 to 0.4. Trading in the second session was light, with the No. 16 bond slightly in demand, and the 1922 bond rose by 0.2 to 0.3, while the rest also improved by 0.1 to 0.2. In the afternoon opening, retail investors sold more, with the 20 bond falling the most, by 0.3 to 0.4, while the rest also fell by a small amount, ranging from 0.1 to 0.2. However, the demobilization bond showed a slight improvement of 0.05 or 0.1. The situation was chaotic, and trading at the close was light, with the trend slightly disordered. Silkworm Rearing Flourishes in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

(Yixing) In recent years, farmers have repeatedly failed in silkworm rearing, and the rural economy has collapsed. Everywhere, there are people who cannot afford to raise silkworms this year. In addition, it is difficult to borrow silkworm capital. Therefore, silkworm farmers have borrowed capital from township offices to purchase improved breeds for rearing, but the amount of rearing has been greatly reduced. The areas of Fufeng Bridge, Baojia Village, Heqiao, Caoqiao, Songdu, Nandu, Lidu, Guancun, Yiziyu, Yangxiang, Xushe, and Qingbaili are relatively smooth. Statistics show that the number of silkworms reared has decreased by about one-third compared to last year. Fortunately, the weather is sunny and warm, and the silkworms are developing well. With the help of instructors, they are developing smoothly. The early batches have completed their third molt and are feeding on leaves. Some are entering their fourth molt. The next batches have just completed their third molt and are feeding on leaves. The latest silkworms are only in their second molt and have been feeding on leaves for three or four days. The current situation is excellent.

(Nanxun) This is a famous area for producing silk thread. In the past, the Silkworm Sericulture Improvement Association sent graduates to establish guidance stations in nearby villages, distribute improved breeds, and guide rearing according to law. Therefore, the results have been remarkable in the past, and farmers have deep faith in improved breeds. The amount of rearing has increased this year, with almost all farmers rearing improved breeds. The weather is sunny and warm, and the silkworms are developing even better. The early batches are about to emerge from their third molt, while the next batches have been feeding on leaves for many days after their second molt. The latest batches are still in their first molt and feeding on leaves. If the weather does not change afterwards, the spring cocoon harvest is expected to increase compared to last year.

Sui'an Zhen Mei Tea Slightly Firms and Rises

Yesterday, in the Shanghai tea market, the British firms Tongfu and Xiehe were still very interested in Zhen Mei green tea from Sui'an. Because of the lack of inventory in the market and the scarcity of supply, selling prices have risen slightly compared to before. Local Zhen Mei tea is also quite popular. However, because raw tea prices in the production areas were expensive before, and foreign firms were closed and did not open the market, tea factories have purchased very little. Therefore, there have been no large new samples released in recent days, resulting in supply not meeting demand. However, the Wenzhou Zhen Mei tea market is slightly weak.

Amateur Chat

"Unemployment and Heartbreak"

— Pu

"Unemployment and Heartbreak" was the topic that Mr. Cai Zimin, a veteran of the party and the nation, spoke about at the inaugural meeting of the "Shishi Club," 丨 an organization that evolved from a dinner party for discussing current events into a formal public organization 丨. As a reporter, I had the privilege of participating in the final seat and was fortunate to hear his famous remarks. Now I am very willing to share what I heard and my thoughts with the readers.

Mr. Cai analyzed the topic itself in great detail. He said: "Unemployment and heartbreak, on the surface, are very common problems in society, and not any specialized major problems such as politics or economics. However, their importance is precisely the fundamental object that all thinkers of education, politics, economics, and sociology, both ancient and modern, want to solve and study. But until now, this problem has not only not been solved, but also has an increasingly difficult appearance to solve. When we look at what is published in the newspapers, whether it belongs to political and economic news or the content of entertainment-oriented movies, they all directly or indirectly express the urgent need to solve this problem and reveal that the situation of 'unemployment and heartbreak' is expanding and tending to be out of control around the world..." Mr. Cai said that the only way to improve the future of these two problems is to maintain the current system. He believes that "unemployment" is a direct result of the current poor political and production systems in various countries; while "heartbreak" is a natural phenomenon formed by the family system centered on traditional thoughts and habits. Finally, he said: "But we see that the national crisis is becoming more and more serious, and at the same time, the number of unemployed and heartbroken people is also increasing. It seems impossible for us to call on these people to pay attention to the issue of national salvation. This is very worthy of our discussion and thought. I specially brought it up today to discuss with the gentlemen of the 'Shishi Club'. It is really not appropriate to call it a speech."

The reporter agrees with what Mr. Cai said in principle, but has a different sentiment regarding seeking solutions to "unemployment and heartbreak." We feel that the solution to this problem (unemployment and heartbreak) cannot be preemptively planned by benevolent gentlemen who already have food and lovers. It must await the masses of "unemployed and heartbroken" people to seek, fight, desperately, and sacrifice themselves after universal awareness, in order to enter the path of liberation.

However, the "unemployed and heartbroken" do not necessarily have to hate the "employed and loved." The common enemy of the "unemployed and heartbroken" is the system that causes "unemployment and heartbreak" and the few system "rulers" who hinder the "unemployed and heartbroken" from seeking liberation.

My "Extra Income" in Life

— Gensheng

Pastry Vendor

That morning, at half past four, when the first whistle of the cotton mill sounded, I got up and started a vigorous fire with the white charcoal in the stove. I placed it under the pan, smeared some lard on the pan, and then placed the pastries on it. Soon, a crackling sound started to emerge. By the time the third whistle of the cotton mill sounded, I quickly took out the steamer, attached the pan in front, and formed a carrying pole – a pastry vendor's pole. I carried it out the back door and headed to the entrance of the cotton mill. Many vendors – some selling sesame cakes and fried dough sticks, some selling glutinous rice – were already there, waiting for the cotton mill workers. I joined in the hustle and bustle, shouting, "Two copper coins for a piece, hot lard pastries!" I was truly brave!

I actually shouted like that.

Well, business wasn't bad. In an hour and a half, I sold more than 150 copper coins worth of pastries. Most of the customers were "young girls."

Page 18

The sky gradually brightened, and the cotton mill had closed its doors. There were fewer buyers. "Let's go!" I said to myself, calmed my spirit, and felt unusually happy. So, I carried the pole and walked toward the area of Sibusar Road and Qiewen Road. I loudly sang, "Hot... lard pastries... hey!" The children in the alleys paid the most attention to this sound. They actually ran out, clutching copper coins to buy pastries. Some who didn't have copper coins had to imitate my tune and sing along. Turning corners and walking, the clock struck ten. My body also felt tired, and the charcoal stove took a rest on its own. "It's better to go back!" I estimated in my mind, "Let's go! Let's go!" I returned home, cooked two bowls of rice, a piece of preserved bean curd, spending eight copper coins for the side dish. After eating my fill and resting a little, I washed three pieces of clothing. It was almost half past one. So, I tidied up my apron, picked up the pole again, and ran towards Qiewen Road, passed Sili Road, Mogan Road, and went up Youdai Corner, earning a few copper coins from the children's hands. As I walked further, I saw a crowd gathered, and a Yangzhou opera was being performed inside a house: a mother and daughter, singing with great enthusiasm, sometimes pretending to cry, sometimes pretending to laugh. I didn't expect them to have such moving art. So I took advantage of this opportunity and sold a lot of pastries. "Two copper coins for a piece, hot lard pastries!"

The sun gradually set. I thought there would be a batch of business to do at the entrance of the cotton mill, because they would be off work at half past five, so I quickly picked up the pole and went there, resting the pole on the latter part of × Tun Road, waiting. Two children were circling around my pastry tray, looking very eager to eat pastries, but they didn't have any copper coins in their hands. One was very cute, so I took a piece of pastry and divided it between the two children. They were extremely happy. A little girl next to them saw it and shouted, "××! ×× (the children's names) are eating the pastry seller's pastries!" Sure enough, the children's older sister ran out, followed by their mother.

"××! Do you have no shame?" Their mother shouted like this.

"It doesn't matter, the amount is limited!" I replied at the same time.

They said, pulling the children and going inside. The man-eating monster's sound in the cotton mill roared again, and the side door opened, and thousands upon thousands of laborers squeezed out, pushing each other. I hurriedly picked up the pole and tried to do business, but those who inquired were few and far between, because they were preparing to go home to cook dinner and didn't need this snack. In the morning, because they had to rush to work on time, they didn't have time to cook, so they just ate some snacks in a hurry. According to the factory rules, it is not allowed to go to work after the deadline. This is the experience I gained.

It was almost six o'clock. I packed up the entire pole and went home. There was some leftover lunch, so I cooked some rice porridge to eat. Under the lamp, I calculated that I had sold more than a hundred pieces of pastry in the morning and afternoon, totaling more than three hundred copper coins. After paying the pastry shop owner two hundred and twenty-five, there was still a surplus of seventy-odd. This was the reward for today, barely enough for two meals of plain rice. Of course, the risk of being caught by the patrol police and taken to the station to be "fined" was not included in this calculation. It would be unfortunate if I suddenly developed heat rash on the road. As for the news material I obtained, that was naturally my "extra income."

Lu Genrong

— Muyin

Factory Manager

Lu Genrong hid behind the machine, his eyes darting around alertly. Between the middle finger and index finger of his right hand, he held a burning cigarette. Wisps of green smoke rose, circling unapologetically into the air. Lu Genrong frequently took long drags, blowing them away.

"Factory Manager!" Wan Afu warned softly from the side. Lu Genrong quickly stubbed out the cigarette, quickly stuffing it into his blue cloth pocket. Looking up, the Factory Manager's small mustache was already visible in front of the machine where he was working. The two piercing, rat-like eyes gave Lu Genrong a chilling terror.

"What's your employee number?" The Factory Manager asked simply.

"I don't have... Factory Manager..."

"The no-smoking sign isn't there for nothing! Dismissal for violators. No need to waste words. Quickly get out your employee card!"

"I wasn't smoking, Factory Manager!" Although Lu Genrong hated his poor luck today, because the cigarette butt wasn't completely extinguished, the green smoke from his pocket was still rising straight up, but he had to stubbornly deny it.

Folk Sayings

The Reason Why "Labor" Cannot Be "Sacred"

— Lu Zhen

It seems that revolution is for the benefit of the masses, so the so-called revolutionary figures are full of clichés like "revolution for the masses, sacrifice for the masses"; targeting the importance of labor, the four words "Labor is Sacred" are shouted even more loudly: it seems that without this, it is not enough to talk about revolution. After all, those who engage in revolution must have a timely golden signboard.

When "Labor is Sacred" was sung to the skies, it was precisely when the revolutionary tide was on the rise, and the revolution had not yet succeeded.

Now, it is said that the revolution has succeeded, but what we see is that "labor" does not seem very "sacred". Or in some places, you can still hear some voices close to "Labor is Sacred", but they are no longer coming from the mouths of those so-called revolutionary figures. Even if they sometimes release it from their mouths with a "poof," it is only limited to a "poof"!

So we can truly assert: "Labor is Sacred," besides being used as a golden signboard, is a check that has never been cashed. If you say otherwise, please look to the facts. The ancients said, "The sacred is inviolable" (human beings today also say this), knowing that the so-called "sacred" implies the meaning of inviolability. But the current "labor" is indeed violable. Where is the "sacredness"? Moreover, the people who violate labor are the same people who sang "Labor is Sacred" before the revolution succeeded!

Some say that whether something is "sacred" or not depends entirely on the conditions it possesses. For example, the "labor" of the past was revolutionary, so it should be "sacred", while the "labor" of today is counter-revolutionary, so it should not be "sacred". As for the criteria for revolution and counter-revolution, the interests of the simultaneous rulers should be used as a guide. For example, if you have a conflict of interest with the ruler, it is counter-revolution; conversely, it is revolution. Therefore, the Great Qing Empire and the Northern Warlords regarded "Sun" and "Huang" as traitors, while the current rulers respect them as revolutionary founders, just like revolutionary figures say that the "labor" of the past was revolutionary, while the present is counter-revolutionary. Understanding this, then the fact that the current "labor" is not "sacred" is not accidental.

Dear "laborers," do you also want to be a little more "sacred"? If you do, you must consider the interests of the current rulers. As for suffering a little "oppression" and a little "exploitation," it doesn't matter. Even if you can't survive, you must absolutely endure and implement "labor-capital cooperation" and strive to "increase production," otherwise, you will be suspected of being counter-revolutionary and cannot be "sacred."

Page 19

The green smoke was still rising outwards, but he had to stubbornly deny it.

"Haha... Ha!" The Factory Manager laughed like a strange owl. "Take it out quickly, or your clothes will catch fire."

Lu Genrong knew that he could no longer argue, so he had to beg the Factory Manager for mercy. At the same time, he thought of his mother and wife at home, and he couldn't help but kneel in front of the Factory Manager.

"Get up! Get up! This is useless. I can't break the factory rules for you alone. If you don't report your employee number, I'll check it myself."

The Factory Manager walked angrily to the office.

The Deputy Factory Manager, sitting at the desk opposite the Factory Manager, was smoking a Bai Jin Long cigarette. Seeing the Factory Manager come in, he engaged him in conversation:

"Chinese cigarettes are ultimately no good. Today I'm trying this Bai Jin Long, the tobacco leaves are much worse than Little Club."

"Well, Chinese merchants are best at cheating, so nothing good can be manufactured!"

The Factory Manager relied on his own theory, so he didn't smoke Chinese cigarettes. He slowly lit his pipe, answering the Deputy Factory Manager while checking Lu Genrong's employee number.

The office door opened. The foreman, accompanying Lu Genrong, had just taken a step in when the Deputy Factory Manager's half-smoked Bai Jin Long was "hissed!" and sacrificed in the spittoon. After all, he was the real Factory Manager. The pipe was only temporarily placed on the side of the table.

"This is his first offense, and he has five family members, big and small, who rely on him to support them. Please, Factory Manager, have mercy and reduce his punishment!" The foreman pointed to Lu Genrong, pleading with the Factory Manager. Lu Genrong hid behind the foreman, watching the Factory Manager's face with hopeful eyes.

"Good! You're interceding for him? Let me ask you, what are you supposed to do as foreman? If workers' violations have to be discovered by me, then what else can we do all day? To be honest, I found this. If the Premier were to come to the factory and see it, you and I would both be in trouble! Since you're pleading for him, you can find him another job yourself. I don't need him here from tomorrow on!" The Factory Manager said a set of words. The foreman rolled his eyes and left without saying a word, leaving Lu Genrong alone, standing there like a wooden chicken.

"Aren't you leaving?" The Deputy Factory Manager seemed to regret his half-smoked Bai Jin Long and shouted as well. So Lu Genrong left with tears in his eyes. At the same time, two more matches were struck in the office, and the fragrant green smoke filled the room.

Amateur Coffee Shop

Pawnbroker's Face

— Jingxian

Working hard from the 1st until the end of the month, the boss looks so pitiful, like a charitable enterprise, digging out snow-white silver dollars from the bulging bag to pay salaries. Although it doesn't draw blood, after selling a month's worth of sweat and getting these salaries, to the boss, it is already extremely generous, but to us small employees, although we feel the pain of "not full, not starving," alas, heavens!... So every time our boss, who married three concubines, pays salaries, I always block the opening of my pocket on the way home, afraid that I will meet a friend with more than one hand than me, like Japan supporting "Manchukuo," coming to plan for the silver dollars in my pocket. Arriving home safely, my wife's face blossomed with smiles, planning to make a velvet cheongsam, preparing to go to Suzhou for a wedding banquet. My son jumped up and down, clamoring to donate two dollars to buy an "Aviation Save the Nation" badge. With great difficulty, I coaxed and deceived, resolving them one by one. I moved out the thirteen-level abacus passed down by my great-grandfather, and clack clack, calculating and calculating, rent, rice money, oil, salt, sauce, vinegar, tuition, favors, everything, exactly offset each other. A whim came to mind, and a flash of inspiration, oh no, the due interest hasn't been settled yet. The creditor's face is really terrible, what to do! Scratching my head, I couldn't think of a way, only to go to the "uncle's house inside the high walls."

Once I had the "determination," I moved forward towards the "consistent policy." Snatching sparrows and digging for rats, long gowns and short jackets, I packed a bundle, sneaking and dodging, afraid of being seen, I slipped into the ×× pawnshop, "eighteen months to full, five days of interest per month." Holding the bundle high in both hands, I placed it on the high counter like a storyteller offering tea. Poor people always run into bad luck, there was no coincidence. The pawnbroker just sat down to eat. The pawnshop rule is that the pawnbroker won't put down his rice bowl, no matter how urgent you are, it's useless. The pawnbroker I encountered was, of course, no exception. After he talked, said, laughed, and ate, enduring for twenty minutes, I thought, here it comes. Who knew that he wouldn't even give me a proper look, shouting to step aside, to wash his face and smoke a water pipe. After everything was done, he reluctantly opened my bundle. Looking far away in another direction, he said, "How much?" I quickly said, "Write thirty dollars." "All old, worth ten dollars at most." He pushed the clothes out while saying this. I wanted to say something, but he had already impatiently said, "Go pawn it somewhere else!" Saying that, he lifted up his water pipe again, not bothering to pay attention to me anymore.

This is called a "Pawnbroker's Face." This is an even uglier face than the imperial army massacring innocent civilians. But the fact tells us that recently, ordinary merchants imitate the "Pawnbroker's Face" in five or six out of ten cases, unless the customer who comes is a modern woman, or an "upper-class person" spewing out of a car. The bosses are doing their best to uphold the slogan of "attentive service." Unfortunately, the small clerks, who "can't die of hunger, can't eat their fill," think of the scene of "wife weeping with hunger, children crying in the cold," think of the embarrassment of going to appreciate the "Pawnbroker's Face," and are really unable to naturally suppress their irritable emotions, forming an unteachable "Pawnbroker's Face." It is true that it is "unreasonable" for small clerks to treat customers with a "Pawnbroker's Face," and it is necessary to "emphasize merchant education," "treat customers with politeness," but, alas, heavens,... What more can be said!

Amateur Education

Reading Club

— Shaoyun

Among the average shop assistants, many are those who had to switch to the commercial world halfway due to family poverty and the inability to continue their studies. Although they no longer have the possibility of returning to school, their desire for knowledge is still very strong. In order to satisfy their desire for knowledge, they need to use their spare time to study on their own. But for self-study, the most difficult thing is: when you don't understand something, there is no one to ask, or you can't find out if your own understanding of a certain issue is correct. If you gather several friends who like to study like yourself and organize a reading club, then the above difficulties can be solved, because in this way, everyone can often study and discuss each other.

The reading club should ideally hold a meeting once a week to discuss difficult points in the books they are reading, or to discuss views on a certain issue. Because in many cases, what one person cannot solve can be resolved to a considerable extent after several people's discussion.

In addition to holding discussion meetings, debate meetings can also be held regularly, finding several debatable issues from the books they have read, or taking the more important issues seen in the newspaper, assigning certain members to argue for the positive side, and certain members to argue for the negative side, and holding a meeting to debate. This can train the organization of the mind, cultivate eloquent speech, and help oneself understand certain issues. Or, after everyone has finished reading a certain book, each person reports on their心得 reading that book, and their criticism of that book; because everyone has different opinions on a certain book, debates can also be conducted based on this type of report and criticism.

In order to increase the interest and progress of reading, academic lecture meetings can be held regularly, inviting people with rich knowledge to give lectures on academic or other practical issues. Before holding this meeting, each member must first have their own views on the issue to be lectured on, and then after listening to the lecture, they can compare it with their own views. If there is anything that is not understood, it can also be asked on the spot.

The reading club also has a good advantage, that is, saving money. For example, Member A buys a book "How to Study New Social Sciences", and Member B can buy "How to Study Emerging Literature" or other books, and everyone can exchange them and read them in turns. If a certain book is something that every member must have a copy of, then in the name of the reading club, buying several copies of the same book can get a discount of 10% or 20% off the marked price.

If the reading club is organized in a large store or factory, then a regular club publication can also be produced, and the content is to publish articles, book and newspaper introductions and criticisms, and reading notes. As for printing, those with economic means can use mimeograph, otherwise copying a copy and posting it on the wall is also possible.

× × ×

Summarizing what is said above, we can draft a specific organizational outline below:

(1) Members: This club is composed of those who are interested in studying a certain science (literature, social sciences or natural sciences, etc.).

(2) Membership fee: Each member pays a membership fee of × yuan per × month.

(3) Club affairs: The main club affairs are:

A. Eight-tenths of the membership fees collected will be used to purchase newspapers for members to read in turns. The remaining funds will be used as office expenses.

B. Divide into groups according to members' preferences for a certain science. For example, those who like form a literary group. (Most people recommend)

C. Each group holds a discussion meeting once a week to solve difficult points in books or on a certain issue.

D. Each group holds a debate meeting once a month to debate academic or other practical important issues. Debaters are taken in turn by the members of each group; the topic is jointly decided by the debaters.

E. Each group may hold academic lecture meetings at any time. The date, location, and lecturer will be notified to all members in advance by the group leader of each group.

F. Issue a club report once every ten days (or every half month). The content is divided into (1) articles, (2) new book introductions and criticisms, (3) reading notes, (4) publishing and literary news, (5) records of discussion meetings, etc., (6) club affairs reports...columns.

(4) Staff: Staff are elected publicly once every six months:

A. Book purchasing director: Responsible for keeping the club's book purchase funds and purchasing books and newspapers on a monthly basis.

B. Book management director: Responsible for keeping the books and newspapers purchased by the club, stipulating the order and time limit for each member to read the books and newspapers in turn, etc.

C. General affairs director: Edits the club report and handles all other affairs.

D. Group leaders of each group: Each group has one group leader, who is responsible for convening various meetings (as for the chairman of the meeting, it is taken in turn by each member.)

(5) Supplementary rules: When this club must be temporarily or permanently disbanded, all books and newspapers will be divided equally among the members.

× × × ×

However, the above-drafted outline is only general. If the number of people is small, it can naturally be modified according to the actual situation.

Small People's Parliament

How Should Workers Maintain Their Livelihoods When Silk Factories Reduce Labor?

— Discussion by Councilor A-Zhen

In last week's "Little People's Assembly," a proposal in French reminded me of a few important points. I am also a silk factory worker.

What we see in the newspapers, besides the Soviet Union, whether it's the old imperialist British Empire, the emerging "Yankee brand," the victorious "France," or the "red scars" who use airplanes, cannons, and poison gas to talk about "friendship" with my "of the same race" country, and the recent Germany with the imperial swastika flag, … all are filled with unemployed and starving masses, especially us workers. Whether East or West, we cannot maintain even a life standard similar to that of cattle and horses.

At this time, who do we workers look to to solve this problem? The International Labor Office of the League of Nations in Geneva? Everyone knows that it is just a few big ocean hooligans putting on a show for some backward worker masses. Petitioning the powerful? When has a petition ever been successful? Moreover, detectives, police, informants, enforcers, labor traitors, etc., are constantly monitoring us. Any "movement" is "rebellious," and extremely dangerous. Kowtowing and begging for pity from the factory owners? That is even more foolish. Capitalists in their cars, mansions, and with their concubines simply won't pity us slaves.

"For the benefit of all our workers, what is the right thing to do?" I think someone will definitely ask me this.

To put it bluntly, all past facts have taught us that there is only one way out:

Unity is strength. All workers unite, organize their own labor unions, oppose labor traitors to deceive and sabotage, oppose non-workers who claim to be leaders, oppose layoffs, oppose capitalists attacking us workers, and strive to protect our livelihoods.

Special self-employment introduction

"Half-Mother's" Tragic Cry

— Ms. Pan Yongliu

I never expected my situation to become so terrible, and even more, I didn't expect that after graduating from high school, I wouldn't be able to find a place to make a living! Indeed! I have tasted the bitterness and joy of life. Last year's life as an elementary school teacher for one semester had already exhausted me, but the meager pay given by the stingy principal couldn't even solve my personal food and clothing problems. But now, I am not seeking or envying the lives of those ladies or modern misses, but struggling for survival, I had to leave everything in my hometown and run alone to this vast city. Deep in my heart, I held a twelve-thousand-fold enthusiasm and hope, hoping that I would not become a starving ghost on the road of life. However, until now, the lesson that reality has taught me is to never again indulge in that illusory dream. I don't even know how I have spent the time in this attic room this past month! Although sometimes I wander by the noisy road, but when I see the smiles of those leisurely people, the proud expressions of the ladies and misses, and the majestic sound of the flowing cars, my heart is filled with infinite sorrow and resentment. Driven and pushed by life, I have also searched all the friends I know, but the answers they gave me were mostly just a few indifferent words like "there is no way." This made me terrified of my future life. I thought, if this kind of life continues, wouldn't I become a lonely soul in a foreign land? Alas! Is this my destiny? In the past, I absolutely did not believe in the so-called fatalism, but now, the reflection that reality has given me makes me have to doubt it, and even more makes me unbearable, especially the innocent little life in my womb for seven months, does he also have any sin? If it continues like this, won't I be implicating him? Alas! Every time I think of this, the tears in my eyes are like a raging wave of ten thousand feet, surging out! In the past, I really couldn't have foreseen that the current society is such a picture, and even more so misshapen. The pain given to me by unemployment has made me deeply recognize and understand all the truths of the current society. But alas! The current predicament │ │ the little life in my womb is getting bigger day by day, can I still sit here and wait for death? Is there really no place in this vast society for me to make a living? In order to solve the problem of childbirth and current life, as long as I can find a job of twenty yuan a month, that is my only hope for survival. Based on the skills that education and society have given me in the past, such as: clerk, home tutor, proofreader, etc., I can do all of them, and I can also write short stories. To put it nicely, I am willing to serve the society wholeheartedly; to put it bluntly, I am willing to exchange my mental labor for this twenty yuan of living expenses. Gentlemen who need this mental labor, please reply in this journal.

Movie Special

Concerts in Movie Theaters

— Lingshan

New Entertainment in the Grand Opening of the Grand Theater

Before the Grand Theater was renovated, it used to rent out one performance every Sunday night to the Public Concession Municipal Council Orchestra to hold concerts. Now, the movies at the Grand Theater have not yet opened, but the concerts have already started last Sunday. However, what they used to play was entirely Western music, so the audience, except for a few music lovers, were all foreigners.

Recently, a Russian composer named Avraam Avraamovich, relying on ten years of experience studying Chinese opera in China, created a kind of Chinese-Western hybrid opera. He said that Chinese music has very rich and beautiful rhythms. It is a pity that the music style is short and there are too many variations, which makes people feel bored. If Western composition methods such as harmony, counterpoint, and modulation can be used to turn Chinese folk songs into long symphonies, it will definitely have a very good effect. Thus, the Fourth Symphony "Impressions of Hutongs in Beijing" and the mime "Qin Xin Bo Guang" and other songs were realized from his ideals!

It is said that these two pieces will be performed by the Municipal Council String Orchestra at the Grand Theater on the 21st of this month. The orchestra will be conducted by Dr. Mei Baiqi, and the mime will be directed by Mei Lanfang │ it is said that Mr. Mei is also preparing to show his face │ · The performers are Tang Xiya, Tang Hui, and film actress Yuan Meiyun and several students from Yucai Public School. This kind of novelty can be regarded as one of the best embellishments in the grand opening of the Grand Theater.

Mr. Avraamovich also believes that Chinese musical instruments have too narrow a range and crude construction, making it difficult to express deep emotions. But,

If foreign musical instruments are used exclusively, there is no way to show the special timbre of Chinese musical instruments, so he advocates a combination of Chinese and Western styles, combining Chinese silk and bamboo drums and cymbals with Western musical instruments. Therefore, this performance can be said to be an unprecedented event. It will add a unique color to the Chinese opera scene. Mr. Avraamovich has many powerful people enthusiastically supporting him behind him. After the performance of this play, he is also preparing to organize a troupe to reform national opera, so that Mr. Avraamovich can concentrate on writing to realize his entire plan.

Film Review

Review of "New Year's Eve"

— Ling He

New Year's Eve, the end of the year, is a solemn and cruel picture in the real Chinese society. Therefore, using this New Year's Eve as the theme of the movie is naturally very novel and appropriate. If we can deeply understand society and grasp the economic significance of the development of that real society, then we can have a thorough solution to this complex problem. However, in this "New Year's Eve" picture, we can only be told the surface of this phenomenon. It explains that the rich people dance, drink, are jealous, fight, and waste money on New Year's Eve, and at the same time it also explains that the poor people have no money to deal with creditors, sell their children, and even commit suicide in this year-end blizzard. But what is the conclusion? "People's hearts are not as they used to be," "the world is deteriorating," and the old scholar still has to give generously at his own life-and-death juncture, and the usurious money shop owner is also willing to do good deeds.

Obviously, "New Year's Eve" does not have a deep understanding of the economic structure. It does not understand the exploitative relationship of usury at all, so it has to ask the rich to be merciful to save people in need. As a result, there is an old scholar with a typical old moral character who gives away the money he got from pawning his daughter "generously and without expecting anything in return" to others (and he is still a gentleman who does not pick up lost items). Of course, these are all characters from the Country of Gentlemen in "Flowers in the Mirror." This kind of unrealistic plot uses old morality to solve this serious social problem.

As mentioned above, this script is indeed very problematic.

However, I cannot ignore the progress of director Jiang Qifeng. Not only in terms of consciousness, he is gradually embarking on a new path, but also in terms of technique, most of it also makes us feel satisfied. He presents this relatively complex plot on the screen in a very orderly manner, and the entire picture is very beautiful. However, the plot is not tense enough, and there is no obvious climax. Although it should be a tragedy that teaches people to cry, it cannot move people's emotions. It can be said that there is a lack of inspiration. The most important thing is that he does not have a strict analysis of the personality of each character. For example, since Jiang Junchao is a righteous and brave young man who fights for justice in the play, he should be a resolute and strong character who would never commit suicide out of cowardice because of three hundred yuan. Then, he suddenly becomes brave again and instead persuades the old scholar to "struggle," which is very contradictory. As for the other actors, they are all properly directed. In terms of performance, Chen Yanyan is the most realistic and successful. Liu Jiqun plays a loyal old man here, which is much more appropriate than the humorous roles he plays. He Feiguang failed. Xing Shaomei is good.

There are other loopholes, such as flipping out a lot of banknotes in the tram in front of everyone, and being able to see the content of the dance hall on the road, Liu Jiqun holding the banknotes and not being afraid of others robbing him at all.

However, there is one characteristic of this play, and that is the success of the photography. This is rare in domestic films. There are few and appropriate subtitles. The setting also suits the plot.

In short, if we don't have to be too demanding on domestic films, then this is a work above the standard.

How are Naval Battle Movies Filmed?

— Donglin

Most of the audience who have seen foreign naval battle movies think that they are taken from the actual scene; this method of photography is not only unreasonable, but also very uneconomical. Moreover, Europe and the United States, where the art of photography has reached the perfect state, how can they not adopt the most economical and practical method? I think there must be many readers who want to understand this photography method that they have always regarded as a mystery! Therefore, I specially wrote this article to share with you readers.

At present, in European, American and Japanese countries, naval battle movies are mostly made with a mechanical, very large rectangular bucket, with very small warship models floating on the water. As long as the mechanism on the side of the bucket is turned, the bucket of water will surge like the ocean during a naval battle. The small warships also shake because of this. Looking from afar, it looks like they are actually fighting in the ocean. The photographer takes this scene, adds a little embellishment, and that is the so-called scene of naval battle. Seeing it with your own eyes is still a bit similar, so don't blame you for watching it in the cinema after so many procedures, thinking that it was taken from the actual scene!

As for the planes flying on the warships, that's even more ridiculous; it's just a toy plane hanging on a thin rope and swinging on a bamboo pole. The audience cannot see through the illusion because the photographer's skill makes it so.

The above is just the long shot of the naval battle movie; as for the close-up shots, the characters taken are not really riding on real warships. That warship is made of wooden boards and iron bars, a part of the real warship. Where is the sea on all sides? Because the lighting is properly arranged, you didn't notice it. The rushing seawater is poured in from above and below!

Although a good method must go hand in hand with good art to achieve true success, so good photography art is indispensable here. Otherwise, it will be like "drawing a tiger but resembling a dog."

The Nanjing Road Continental Department Store China National Products Company held a fashion show to promote national fashion. Mayor Wu's wife also attended, and famous ladies from Shanghai also came. More than a dozen movie stars, including Hu Die, Hu Ping, and Xu Lai, joined the fashion show, which won a lot of praise. This is a picture of Ms. Hu Die's new outfit.

Charlie Chaplin's Quirks

— Mu Zhu

Chaplin has a strange habit that is different from others in his life. His romantic behavior is simply unparalleled, probably based on his innate peculiarity and cultivated. No one probably understands his character except his wife (now separated) and his subordinates. Obstinate, cautious, stubborn, dissolute, and fanatical are the collections of several conflicting personalities that make up Chaplin's entire personality. On a certain day of filming, when the work was at its most intense, Chaplin said to his subordinates: "I'm too tired! Let's go to Europe for a walk." When they heard this, they immediately stopped all work and quickly packed their luggage for their master: because they had seen through the master's quirk. The next day, Chaplin really set off for Europe. From the perspective of ordinary people, don't you think Chaplin's quirk is strange? Also, Chaplin has a magnificent swimming pool built in his house, but he has never taken the plunge. One day, he was inexplicably happy, immediately changed his clothes, jumped into the pool and swam wildly, until he could no longer tremble, before he called someone to carry him to bed, and then said it was fun. These are just a few random facts, but they are enough to prove Chaplin's top-notch quirks. It is said that he has had as many as seven past lovers and divorced wives. Recently, the heroine of "Waterloo Bridge," Pola Negri, also had a love affair with him. What a blessing for Chaplin! Unfortunately, one after another, they broke up or divorced, causing a stir in the city. In the end, he is still a single man. Now it seems that he wants to try the taste of marriage again, and the opponent has also been found, but she may not have noticed the benefits of Chaplin. It is rumored that Chaplin is planning to shoot "Napoleon," intending to direct and play the leading role himself. Maybe he simply won't participate in the role and find someone else to do it. But when will this lucky character be found?

Why Wear Skirts?

— Wu Qingfen

I have seen many Chinese movies, in which older women or old-fashioned middle-aged women are always wearing skirts. This point in my mind raised a question: "Why do they wear skirts?" In China, during the Qing Dynasty, women's formal attire was a long coat and skirt, but it is still popular in the Republic of China era, so you can still see those older women wearing skirts on the street; but you should know that they only wear them when they encounter happy events or visit relatives and friends, and they don't usually wear them at home. But now I see in the movie that skirts are worn even during ordinary conversations between old couples, or usually at home, which seems unreasonable to me. Because movies are realistic, unlike new dramas. (Compensatory)

Secrets of the Movie Novel (Secrets) (8)

— Cairo

Shen Xiang walked away with a heavy heart. He was thinking in his heart, I hope they will still return to the countryside, far away from this colorful crowd. There, there is a rough life and hard work that can keep people on the right path and not have crooked thoughts. In Shen Xiang's heart, which has been through many hardships, this ease in a pile of silks and satins is much more dangerous than country life.

Because John's power is growing day by day, of course there will be a group of people who tend to flatter him. He naturally embarked on the road of politicians, because that is the only destination for those who own wealth and power. For several years, he has been purchasing everywhere, and parades are welcomed everywhere. In addition to a group of men who climb the dragon and attach the phoenix, there is also a group of women with great ambitions to seduce him, and this Miss Martinez is one of them.

Martinez's participation in the dance party at the Carden's house this time was not invited by Carden, she came with great ambition. Mary tried her best to suppress the grief in her heart all night, socializing among the guests, pretending to be generous and dignified. When it was late and the guests were gone, she couldn't hold on any longer. She slipped out alone and ran to a small living room, lying on a sofa, shedding tears. Unexpectedly, Martinez had followed her. Mary heard a low knock on the door outside, and she quickly wiped away her tears and opened the door. This Spanish young woman came in.

After Martinez came in, the two were silent for a long time. They were measuring each other's strength. Finally, Martinez opened her mouth. She said, "My only reason is that I love your husband!"

"That's not possible," Mary said calmly. "If you really treat him sincerely, how could you run to his house so rashly and humiliate him and his wife's family in front of so many guests and friends?"

"I'm very sorry about that. I misunderstood someone else's words. But the fact still exists, that is, I love your husband, and he loves me." As she spoke, Martinez pretended to be very respectful.

"I can't admit that either," Mary said without hesitation. "Of course, my husband was seduced by you, there is no doubt about that. You also look very charming. But that's all. I know my husband well."

"Do you know your husband?" Martinez said in protest? "Your husband needs happiness, freedom, and passion, but you can't provide him with it. You don't understand your husband at all. He needs freedom! But he said you definitely won't let him go."

"My husband... did he say that to you?" Mary said, trying to appear calm.

"Yes."

"He loves you... He wants me to release him so that he can marry you... but I don't agree... did he tell you this?"

"Yes." (To be continued)

— Luo Fen

The recent anti-foreign sentiment in the United States has aroused the resentment of many foreign stars, and they have automatically withdrawn. Recently, within a week, a total of fifteen foreign stars and twenty-eight unsigned actors have left the United States and returned to their hometowns. As for those who are preparing to leave, they are now countless. This is an unprecedented disturbance in Hollywood. Now the US authorities are also very panicked, fearing that Hollywood will feel a lack of talent and cause a business crisis, so the current anti-foreign methods have a motive for improvement.
